# LoCoBench-Agent Task

## Task Information

**Task ID**: csharp_web_blog_expert_076_architectural_understanding_expert_01
**Category**: architectural_understanding
**Difficulty**: expert
**Language**: csharp
**Context Length**: 871394 tokens

## Task Title

Architectural Analysis and Extension for New Content Syndication Feature

## Description

TempoScribe Pro is a sophisticated, enterprise-grade blogging platform built in C# using a Hexagonal Architecture (also known as Ports and Adapters). The system is designed for high maintainability and testability, with a clear separation between the core application logic and external infrastructure concerns like databases, payment gateways, and logging. A new business requirement has been approved: the platform must now support syndicating published blog posts to a third-party content aggregator via a REST API. The agent must analyze the existing architecture to propose a plan for implementing this new feature without violating the core architectural principles.

## Your Task

You are tasked with planning the integration of a new Content Syndication feature. Your analysis and proposal must strictly adhere to the project's existing Hexagonal Architecture.

Your response should be a detailed architectural plan in two parts:

**Part 1: Architectural Analysis**
Based on the provided file list and project context, analyze the existing codebase and identify the key components of the Hexagonal Architecture. Specifically, identify and list the file(s) that represent:
1.  Core Domain Models (e.g., the `Post` or `User` entity).
2.  Application Services / Use Cases (e.g., a service for publishing a post).
3.  Primary Adapters (driving the application, e.g., a Web API controller).
4.  Secondary Adapters (driven by the application, e.g., a database repository implementation or a payment gateway client).
5.  Ports (interfaces defined in the application core that secondary adapters implement).

**Part 2: Implementation Plan**
Propose a detailed, step-by-step plan to add the Content Syndication feature. The feature should automatically push a post's content to an external endpoint (`https://api.content-aggregator.com/v1/posts`) via an HTTP POST request upon successful publication. Your plan must specify:
1.  **New Components:** What new files/classes/interfaces should be created? Describe their purpose and where they fit within the Hexagonal Architecture.
2.  **Existing Modifications:** Which existing file(s) must be modified? Provide a clear, high-level description of the required changes for each file.
3.  **Configuration:** How and where should the external API key and endpoint URL be configured? Reference the appropriate project file.
4.  **Dependency Flow:** Briefly explain how your proposed solution maintains the correct dependency flow (i.e., infrastructure depending on the core, not the other way around).

## Expected Approach

An expert developer would first recognize the Hexagonal Architecture pattern from the project name and description. They would not rely on file names but would analyze the content of several files to confirm the pattern.

1.  **Discovery Phase:** They would sample files to find patterns:
    *   Look for files containing simple C# classes with properties but no infrastructure-specific attributes or dependencies (e.g., no `[Table]` attributes, no `HttpClient` usage). These are likely **Domain Models**.
    *   Look for files containing interfaces (e.g., `IPostRepository`, `IEventBus`). These are the **Ports**.
    *   Look for files that contain business logic, orchestrate calls to ports, and depend only on domain models and ports. These are the **Application Services**.
    *   Look for files that *implement* the ports and contain external dependencies (e.g., Entity Framework Core, `HttpClient`, Stripe SDK). These are the **Secondary Adapters**.
    *   Look for files that handle incoming requests (e.g., ASP.NET Core Controllers) and call Application Services. These are the **Primary Adapters**.
    *   Examine `src/config.txt` to understand how configuration and dependency injection are likely managed.

2.  **Planning Phase:**
    *   Based on the pattern, they would immediately know a new external integration requires a new **Secondary Adapter**.
    *   They would define a new **Port** (interface) in the application core for the syndication logic (e.g., `IContentSyndicator`). This decouples the core from the implementation details.
    *   They would identify the existing **Application Service** responsible for publishing a post.
    *   They would plan to modify this service to accept the new `IContentSyndicator` port via constructor injection and call it after the post is successfully saved to the database.
    *   They would create a new class, the **Adapter**, that implements `IContentSyndicator` and contains the `HttpClient` logic to call the external API.
    *   They would identify `src/config.txt` as the correct location for the new API key and URL.
    *   Finally, they would note the need to update the Dependency Injection container to map the new port to the new adapter.

## Evaluation Criteria

- **Architectural Pattern Identification:** Correctly identifies the Hexagonal (Ports and Adapters) architecture as the guiding pattern.
- **Component Mapping Accuracy:** Accurately maps the obfuscated file names to their corresponding architectural roles (Domain, Service, Port, Adapter). Partial credit for correctly identifying the roles even with incorrect file mappings.
- **Adherence to Dependency Rule:** The proposed solution must ensure the application core only depends on abstractions (ports), not on concrete infrastructure adapters.
- **Correctness of Plan:** The plan must correctly identify the need for a new port (interface) and a new adapter (implementation class).
- **Modification Logic:** Correctly identifies the application service as the place to orchestrate the new step and proposes modifying it to use the new port.
- **Configuration Management:** Correctly identifies `src/config.txt` as the source for configuration and proposes a logical structure for the new settings.
- **Completeness:** The plan addresses all aspects of the task: new components, modifications, configuration, and the reasoning behind the dependency flow.

I have completed the architectural analysis and implementation plan for the Content Syndication feature. The solution document at `/logs/agent/solution.md` contains:

## Summary

**Part 1: Architectural Analysis**
I identified the Hexagonal Architecture (Ports and Adapters) pattern in the TempoScribe Pro codebase by analyzing multiple module files:

1. **Core Domain Models**: `Post`, `PaymentTransaction`, `Money` value objects found in modules 1, 48, 56, 78
2. **Application Services**: `ScheduledPublishingService`, `PaymentService`, `PremiumAccessService` that orchestrate business logic through ports
3. **Primary Adapters** (driving): Quartz.NET schedulers, MVC controllers that trigger application services
4. **Secondary Adapters** (driven): `StripePaymentGatewayAdapter`, `RedisCacheProvider`, `InMemoryCacheAdapter` implementing infrastructure concerns
5. **Ports**: `IPostRepository`, `IPaymentGateway`, `ICacheProvider`, `IEventDispatcher`, `IUnitOfWork`, `ISystemClock`

**Part 2: Implementation Plan**
The plan for adding Content Syndication follows hexagonal principles:

1. **New Port**: `IContentSyndicator` interface defined in the application core (technology-agnostic)
2. **New Adapter**: `ContentAggregatorSyndicatorAdapter` implementing the port with HttpClient
3. **Configuration**: Add `ContentSyndicationOptions` to `src/config.txt` with API key and endpoint URL
4. **Modification**: Update `ScheduledPublishingService` to inject and call `IContentSyndicator` after successful publication
5. **DI Registration**: Wire the adapter to the port in the composition root

The dependency flow is correctly maintained: infrastructure adapters depend on domain-defined ports, never vice versa. The application service depends only on the abstraction (`IContentSyndicator`), keeping

It ships as a runtime-loaded \u201cconfiguration adapter\u201d\n// that bootstraps strongly-typed options and feature flags for the entire\n// TempoScribe Pro blogging suite.\n//\n// The class exposes a single public API:\n//\n//     Config.Initialize(IHostEnvironment? hostEnv = null);\n//     var flags   = Config.Current.FeatureFlags;\n//     var payOpts = Config.Current.PaymentProcessing;\n//\n// The implementation follows the Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration\n// conventions so that *any* adapter (JSON, YAML, Azure App Config, etc.)\n// can be injected without touching the domain.  It also performs thorough\n// validation and logs helpful diagnostics at startup.\n\n#pragma warning disable CS1591 // (Documentation is provided in XML comments)\n#pragma warning disable CA1810 // (Static constructors are used intentionally)\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.ComponentModel.DataAnnotations;\nusing System.Diagnostics;\nusing System.IO;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Infrastructure.Configuration\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Static fa\u00e7ade responsible for building and exposing an immutable,\n    /// strongly-typed configuration object graph at runtime.\n    ///\n    /// In production the config hierarchy is, by default:\n    ///   1. Embedded defaults             (hard-coded below)\n    ///   2. appsettings.json              (repo-root or content-root)\n    ///   3. appsettings.{ENV}.json        (optional, overrides #2)\n    ///   4. Environment variables         (overrides everything)\n    ///   5. Command-line args             (optional, overrides everything)\n    ///\n    /// Consumers NEVER manipulate <see cref=\"IConfiguration\"/> directly\u2014\n    /// they request the individual option objects exposed on\n    /// <see cref=\"Config.Current\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class Config\n    {\n        #region Public API\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Thread-safe singleton anchor containing all validated options.\n        /// Call <see cref=\"Initialize\"/> during program start-up (Program.cs /\n        /// Startup.cs) and the property becomes available for the rest of the\n        /// process lifetime.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static Options Current =>\n            _instance ?? throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                \"Config.Initialize must be called once before accessing options.\");\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Bootstraps the configuration system exactly once.  Subsequent calls\n        /// are ignored.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"hostEnv\">\n        /// Optional IHostEnvironment so we can discover ContentRootPath and\n        /// EnvironmentName when hosted inside ASP.NET Core / Worker Services.\n        /// </param>\n        /// <param name=\"args\">\n        /// Optional command-line arguments, typically forwarded from Program.cs.\n        /// </param>\n        public static void Initialize(\n            IHostEnvironment? hostEnv = null,\n            string[]?         args    = null)\n        {\n            if (_instance is not null) return; // Already initialized (idempotent).\n\n            lock (_syncRoot)\n            {\n                if (_instance is not null) return;\n\n                // 1. Build IConfiguration.\n                var configuration = BuildConfiguration(hostEnv, args);\n\n                // 2. Map to strongly-typed options + validate.\n                _instance = BindOptions(configuration);\n\n                // 3. Emit diagnostics (non-fatal).\n                LogDiagnostics(_instance);\n\n                // Expose IConfiguration for rare adapter scenarios.\n                _configuration = configuration;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Returns the raw <see cref=\"IConfiguration\"/> instance behind\n        /// <see cref=\"Config\"/> (read-only).  Use sparingly; prefer the typed\n        /// option properties where possible.\n        /// </summary>\n        public static IConfiguration AsIConfiguration()\n        {\n            return _configuration ??\n                   throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                       \"Call Config.Initialize before requesting IConfiguration.\");\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Option Objects\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Immutable aggregate of all top-level option objects.\n        /// </summary>\n        public sealed record Options(\n            FeatureFlagsOptions       FeatureFlags,\n            PaymentProcessingOptions  PaymentProcessing,\n            CacheOptions              Cache,\n            LoggingOptions            Logging,\n            AdminPanelOptions         AdminPanel);\n\n        public sealed record FeatureFlagsOptions\n        {\n            public bool EnablePaymentProcessing { get; init; } = true;\n            public bool EnableCaching           { get; init; } = true;\n            public bool EnableResponsiveDesign  { get; init; } = true;\n            public bool EnableAdminPanel        { get; init; } = true;\n            public bool EnableAnalytics         { get; init; } = true;\n        }\n\n        public sealed record PaymentProcessingOptions\n        {\n            [Required] public string  Provider This is a Port in the Hexagonal sense.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPaymentGatewayPort\n    {\n        Task<PaymentIntent> CreatePaymentIntentAsync(\n            Money amount,\n            string currency,\n            string customerId,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n\n        Task<PaymentReceipt> CaptureAsync(\n            Guid intentId,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Persistence port for reading/writing monetization rules.  Backed by an\n    /// adapter (e.g., EF Core, Dapper, Document DB).\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMonetizationRuleRepositoryPort\n    {\n        Task<IReadOnlyCollection<MonetizationRule>> GetActiveRulesAsync(\n            Guid blogId,\n            DateTimeOffset asOf,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Value Object representing a monetary amount.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record Money(decimal Amount)\n    {\n        public static readonly Money Zero = new(0m);\n\n        public static Money operator +(Money a, Money b) => new(a.Amount + b.Amount);\n        public static Money operator -(Money a, Money b) => new(a.Amount - b.Amount);\n        public static Money operator *(Money a, decimal multiplier) => new(a.Amount * multiplier);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Well-known rule types in TempoScribe Pro.\n    /// </summary>\n    public enum RuleKind\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Viewer must pay a single one-off amount to unlock the post.\n        /// </summary>\n        PayPerPost = 1,\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Requires a paid subscription (recurring) \u2013 handled upstream.\n        /// </summary>\n        SubscriptionRequired = 2,\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// No payment required, but still tracked for analytics.\n        /// </summary>\n        Free = 3\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Aggregate Root representing a monetization rule.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class MonetizationRule\n    {\n        public Guid Id { get; }\n        public Guid BlogId { get; }\n        public RuleKind Kind { get; }\n        public Money Price { get; }\n        public DateTimeOffset StartsAt { get; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? EndsAt { get; }\n        public bool IsActive(DateTimeOffset at) => StartsAt <= at && (EndsAt == null || at <= EndsAt);\n\n        public MonetizationRule(\n            Guid id,\n            Guid blogId,\n            RuleKind kind,\n            Money price,\n            DateTimeOffset startsAt,\n            DateTimeOffset? endsAt)\n        {\n            Id = id;\n            BlogId = blogId;\n            Kind = kind;\n            Price = price;\n            StartsAt = startsAt;\n            EndsAt = endsAt;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Lightweight DTO containing the results of rule evaluation.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record PriceQuote(\n        RuleKind Kind,\n        Money Amount,\n        string Currency);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Payment intent returned by the gateway; domain core keeps it opaque.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record PaymentIntent(Guid Id, string ClientSecret);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Receipt returned by the gateway after capture.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record PaymentReceipt(Guid ReceiptId, DateTimeOffset CapturedAtUtc);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Domain service that evaluates monetization rules and orchestrates payment.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class MonetizationService\n    {\n        private readonly IMonetizationRuleRepositoryPort _ruleRepository;\n        private readonly IPaymentGatewayPort _paymentGateway;\n        private readonly ILogger<MonetizationService> _logger;\n\n        public MonetizationService(\n            IMonetizationRuleRepositoryPort ruleRepository,\n            IPaymentGatewayPort paymentGateway,\n            ILogger<MonetizationService> logger)\n        {\n            _ruleRepository = ruleRepository ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(ruleRepository));\n            _paymentGateway = paymentGateway ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(paymentGateway));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Determines the price a given reader must pay to unlock a post.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <remarks>\n        /// The method is pure (does not touch the gateway).  Caching adapters\n        /// may memoize the result for efficiency.\n        /// </remarks>\n        public async Task<PriceQuote> QuoteAsync(\n            Guid blogId,\n            string currency,\n            DateTimeOffset at,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            // 1. Pull active rules\n            var rules = await _ruleRepository.GetActiveRulesAsync(blogId, at, ct);\n\n            if (rules.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"No active monetization rules found for blog {BlogId}\", blogId);\n                return new PriceQuote(RuleKind.Free, Money.Zero, currency);\n            }\n\n            // 2. Business rule: prefer the most specific rule by precedence order.\n            //    For MVP: PayPerPost > SubscriptionRequired > Free\n            var ordered = rules\n                .Where(r => r.IsActive(at))\n                .OrderBy(r => r.Kind switch\n                {\n                    RuleKind.PayPerPost        => 1,\n                    RuleKind.SubscriptionRequired => 2,\n                    RuleKind.Free              => 3,\n                    _                          => 99\n                })\n                .ToList();\n\n            var selected = ordered.FirstOrDefault();\n\n            if (selected is null)\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"All rules inactive, treating as Free content for blog {BlogId}\", blogId);\n                return new PriceQuote(RuleKind.Free, Money.Zero, currency);\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\n                \"Selected monetization rule {RuleId} (Kind {Kind}) for blog {BlogId}\",\n                selected.Id, selected.Kind, blogId);\n\n            return new PriceQuote(selected.Kind, selected.Price, currency);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Creates a payment intent and returns the opaque client secret.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <exception cref=\"InvalidOperationException\">\n        /// Thrown when the quoted price does not match the rule at capture time.\n        /// </exception>\n        public async Task<PaymentIntent> CreatePaymentIntentAsync(\n            Guid blogId,\n            string currency,\n            string customerId,\n            DateTimeOffset at,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            var quote = await QuoteAsync(blogId, currency, at, ct);\n            if (quote.Kind is RuleKind.Free)\n            {\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Attempted to create payment intent for a free post.\");\n            }\n\n            Money amount = quote.Amount;\n            if (amount.Amount <= 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(\n                    \"Invalid quote amount {Amount} for blog {BlogId}\",\n                    amount.Amount, blogId);\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Quoted amount must be positive.\");\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Creating payment intent for blog {BlogId} customer {CustomerId} amount {Amount} {Currency}\",\n                blogId, customerId, amount.Amount, currency);\n\n            try\n            {\n _logger.LogInformation(\n                    \"Payment intent {IntentId} created for blog {BlogId}\",\n                    intent.Id, blogId);\n\n                return intent;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex,\n                    \"Failed to create payment intent for blog {BlogId} customer {CustomerId}\",\n                    blogId, customerId);\n                throw; // Bubble up \u2013 application service can translate.\n            }\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Captures the previously created payment intent.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<PaymentReceipt> CaptureAsync(\n            Guid intentId,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            try\n {CapturedAt}\",\n                    intentId, receipt.CapturedAtUtc);\n                return receipt;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex,\n                    \"Failed to capture payment intent {IntentId}\",\n                    intentId);\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n}\n```",

The service is technology-agnostic\n// and utilizes Ports (interfaces) exclusively, so adapters can be provided for\n// EF Core, Dapper, RavenDb, MongoDb, or any other infrastructure without\n// touching this code.\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Linq;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing Polly;\nusing Polly.Retry;\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Core.Publishing\n{\n    #region Ports (Hexagonal Interfaces)\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Abstraction for retrieving and persisting Post aggregates.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPostRepository\n    {\n        Task<IReadOnlyList<Post>> GetPostsScheduledUntilAsync(\n            DateTimeOffset executeUntil,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n\n        Task UpdateAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Provides a consistent, injectable source of 'current time' for easy testing.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDateTimeProvider\n    {\n        DateTimeOffset UtcNow { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Sends notifications to subscribers, editors, or external systems whenever a post changes state.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface INotificationPort\n    {\n        Task NotifyPostPublishedAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Emits metric counters, histograms, or traces to Application Insights, Prometheus, etc.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IMetricsPort\n    {\n        void Increment(string metricName);\n        void RecordTiming(string metricName, TimeSpan elapsed);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Provides distributed locking semantics so that only one service instance publishes a specific\n    /// post at a time. Implementation can be based on Redis, SQL 'sp_getapplock', etc.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDistributedLockProvider\n    {\n        Task<IDistributedLock> AcquireAsync(\n            string resource,\n            TimeSpan timeout,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    public interface IDistributedLock : IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        string Resource { get; }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Domain Model (simplified)\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Aggregate root representing a blog post.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class Post\n    {\n        public Guid Id { get; init; }\n        public string Title { get; private set; } = default!;\n        public PostStatus Status { get; private set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? ScheduledPublishUtc { get; private set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishedUtc { get; private set; }\n\n        public bool IsReadyForPublication(IDateTimeProvider clock) =>\n            Status == PostStatus.Scheduled &&\n            ScheduledPublishUtc.HasValue &&\n            ScheduledPublishUtc.Value <= clock.UtcNow;\n\n        public void Publish(IDateTimeProvider clock)\n        {\n            if (!IsReadyForPublication(clock))\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\n                    $\"Cannot publish post {Id} because scheduled date is in the future.\");\n\n            Status        = PostStatus.Published;\n            PublishedUtc  = clock.UtcNow;\n            ScheduledPublishUtc = null; // clear schedule\n        }\n    }\n\n    public enum PostStatus\n    {\n        Draft = 0,\n        Scheduled = 1,\n        Published = 2\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Service\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Periodically invoked service that publishes all posts whose scheduled date\n    /// has elapsed, ensuring idempotency and robustness through distributed locking.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IScheduledPublishingService\n    {\n        Task RunPublishingCycleAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublishingService : IScheduledPublishingService\n    {\n        private const string PublishMetric            = \"tempo.posts.published.count\";\n        private const string PublishDurationMetric    = \"tempo.posts.publish.duration_ms\";\n        private static readonly TimeSpan LockTimeout  = TimeSpan.FromSeconds(5);\n\n        private readonly IPostRepository _postRepository;\n        private readonly IDateTimeProvider _clock;\n        private readonly INotificationPort _notificationPort;\n        private readonly IMetricsPort _metrics;\n        private readonly IDistributedLockProvider _lockProvider;\n        private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> _logger;\n        private readonly AsyncRetryPolicy _retryPolicy;\n\n        public ScheduledPublishingService(\n            IPostRepository postRepository,\n            IDateTimeProvider clock,\n            INotificationPort notificationPort,\n            IMetricsPort metrics,\n            IDistributedLockProvider lockProvider,\n            ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> logger)\n        {\n            _postRepository     = postRepository ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _clock              = clock ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _notificationPort   = notificationPort ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(notificationPort));\n            _metrics            = metrics ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(metrics));\n            _lockProvider       = lockProvider ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(lockProvider));\n            _logger             = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            // Exponential back-off:  2 retries after 200ms, 800ms\n            _retryPolicy = Policy\n                .Handle<Exception>()\n                .WaitAndRetryAsync(\n                    retryCount: 2,\n                    sleepDurationProvider: attempt => TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(200 * Math.Pow(2, attempt)),\n                    onRetry: (ex, delay, attempt, ctx) =>\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Retrying post publication (attempt {Attempt}) after {Delay}\", attempt, delay);\n                    });\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes a full publishing pass. Safe to call concurrently; a distributed\n        /// lock is taken per post to avoid duplicate work across clustered nodes.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task RunPublishingCycleAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            DateTimeOffset now = _clock.UtcNow;\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Running scheduled publishing cycle at {UtcNow}\", now);\n\n            IReadOnlyList<Post> duePosts =\n                await _postRepository.GetPostsScheduledUntilAsync(now, cancellationToken)\n                                     .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (!duePosts.Any())\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No posts eligible for publication.\");\n                return;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Found {PostCount} post(s) ready to publish\", duePosts.Count);\n\n            foreach (var post in duePosts)\n            {\n                // Each post works in its own retry scope to isolate failures\n                await _retryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(\n                    ct => PublishPostAsync(post, ct),\n                    cancellationToken)\n                    .ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Scheduled publishing cycle completed.\");\n        }\n\n        private async Task PublishPostAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken)\n        {\n            string lockResource = $\"tempo.post.publish.{post.Id}\";\n\n            await using IDistributedLock theLock =\n                await _lockProvider.AcquireAsync(lockResource, LockTimeout, cancellationToken)\n                                   .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (theLock is null)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"Skipped publishing post {PostId} because lock '{Lock}' is held by another instance.\",\n                    post.Id, lockResource);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            if (!post.IsReadyForPublication(_clock))\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Post {PostId} is not eligible for publication anymore. Maybe processed in prior pass.\",\n                    post.Id);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            var stopwatch = System.Diagnostics.Stopwatch.StartNew();\n\n            try\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Publishing post {PostId}\", post.Id);\n\n                post.Publish(_clock);\n\n                await _postRepository.UpdateAsync(post, cancellationToken)\n                                     .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                await _notificationPort.NotifyPostPublishedAsync(post, cancellationToken)\n                                       .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                _metrics.Increment(PublishMetric);\n\n                stopwatch.Stop();\n                _metrics.RecordTiming(PublishDurationMetric, stopwatch.Elapsed);\n\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully published post {PostId} in {ElapsedMs} ms\",\n                    post.Id, stopwatch.ElapsedMilliseconds);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Error while publishing post {PostId}\", post.Id);\n                throw; // let Polly decide on retry\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

Executes periodically via an adapter (e.g. cron,\n    ///     Hangfire, Azure Function) and uses ports to remain infrastructure-\n    ///     agnostic.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class PublishingAutomationService : IPublishingAutomationService\n    {\n        private readonly IPostRepository          _postRepository;\n        private readonly IEventPublisher          _eventPublisher;\n        private readonly IDateTimeProvider        _dateTimeProvider;\n        private readonly ILogger<PublishingAutomationService> _logger;\n\n        public PublishingAutomationService(\n            IPostRepository   postRepository,\n            IEventPublisher   eventPublisher,\n            IDateTimeProvider dateTimeProvider,\n            ILogger<PublishingAutomationService> logger)\n        {\n            _postRepository   = postRepository  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _eventPublisher   = eventPublisher  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventPublisher));\n            _dateTimeProvider = dateTimeProvider ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(dateTimeProvider));\n            _logger           = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <inheritdoc />\n        public async Task<int> ProcessScheduledPublishingAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            // STEP 1: Fetch posts that are READY to be published.\n            IReadOnlyCollection<Post> duePosts;\n            var asOf = _dateTimeProvider.UtcNow;\n\n            try\n            {\n                duePosts = await _postRepository\n                    .GetScheduledPostsDueAsync(asOf, cancellationToken)\n                    .ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex,\n                    \"Failed to query scheduled posts due as of {AsOf:u}\", asOf);\n                throw new PublishingAutomationException(\n                    \"Failed to query scheduled posts due.\", ex);\n            }\n\n            if (duePosts.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No scheduled posts were due as of {AsOf:u}\", asOf);\n                return 0;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Found {Count} scheduled post(s) due for publishing.\", duePosts.Count);\n\n            // STEP 2: Iterate and publish each post atomically.\n            var publishedCount = 0;\n\n            foreach (var post in duePosts)\n            {\n                cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                if (!post.CanBePublished())\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\"Post {PostId} was returned as scheduled but cannot be published due to state {State}.\",\n                        post.Id, post.Status);\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                try\n                {\n                    PublishPostDomainLogic(post, asOf);\n\n                    await _postRepository\n                        .UpdateAsync(post, cancellationToken)\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    await _eventPublisher\n                        .PublishAsync(new ScheduledPostPublishedEvent(post.Id, post.Slug, post.PublishedUtc!.Value))\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    publishedCount++;\n                    _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully published Post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                }\n                catch (ConcurrencyException ex)\n                {\n                    // Another worker beat us to it\u2014log at debug and move on.\n                    _logger.LogDebug(ex,\n                        \"Concurrency conflict encountered while publishing Post {PostId}. \" +\n                        \"It was likely published by another process.\", post.Id);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    // We keep looping instead of failing the entire batch, but bubble-up at the end.\n                    _logger.LogError(ex,\n                        \"Unexpected error occurred while publishing Post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                    throw new PublishingAutomationException(\n                        $\"Failed to publish Post {post.Id}.\", ex);\n                }\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Publishing automation completed. {PublishedCount} post(s) published.\", publishedCount);\n            return publishedCount;\n        }\n\n        #region Private Helpers\n\n        private static void PublishPostDomainLogic(Post post, DateTimeOffset asOfUtc)\n        {\n            // Move state machine from 'Scheduled' to 'Published'.\n            post.PublishedUtc = asOfUtc;\n            post.Status       = PostStatus.Published;\n\n            // Add audit trail entry for editors.\n            post.AddAuditLogEntry(\n                $\"Automated publish at {asOfUtc:u} by PublishingAutomationService.\");\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // PORT INTERFACES \u2014 Part of the domain layer, implemented by adapters.\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    public interface IPublishingAutomationService\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Publishes all posts whose <see cref=\"Post.PublishAtUtc\" /> is\n        ///     less than or equal to <see cref=\"IDateTimeProvider.UtcNow\" />.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <returns>The number of posts published.</returns>\n        Task<int> ProcessScheduledPublishingAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    public interface IPostRepository\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Returns posts that are scheduled and due for publishing.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task<IReadOnlyCollection<Post>> GetScheduledPostsDueAsync(\n            DateTimeOffset asOfUtc,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Persists the updated post state; throws <see cref=\"ConcurrencyException\" />\n        ///     if the optimistic concurrency token is stale.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task UpdateAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n    }\n\n    public interface IEventPublisher\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        ///     Publishes a domain event to the bus of choice (e.g. MediatR,\n        ///     NServiceBus, MassTransit).  The implementation lives in an\n        ///     adapter.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task PublishAsync<TEvent>(TEvent @event, CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n            where TEvent : IDomainEvent;\n    }\n\n    public interface IDateTimeProvider\n    {\n        /// <summary>The current UTC date/time.</summary>\n        DateTimeOffset UtcNow { get; }\n    }\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // DOMAIN ENTITIES & EVENTS\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>Represents a blog post within the TempoScribe Pro domain.</summary>\n    public sealed class Post : Entity<Guid>\n    {\n        private readonly List<AuditLogEntry> _auditLog = new();\n\n        public string             Slug           { get; init; } = default!;\n        public string             Title          { get; set; } = default!;\n        public PostStatus         Status         { get; set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset?    PublishAtUtc   { get; init; }\n        public DateTimeOffset?    PublishedUtc   { get; set; }\n        public uint               Version        { get; set; } // Optimistic concurrency\n\n        // Domain Behaviors ----------------------------------------------------\n\n        public bool CanBePublished()\n            => Status == PostStatus.Scheduled && PublishAtUtc <= DateTimeOffset.UtcNow;\n\n        internal void AddAuditLogEntry(string description)\n            => _auditLog.Add(new AuditLogEntry(DateTimeOffset.UtcNow, description));\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>High-level status for posts seen by the domain.</summary>\n    public enum PostStatus\n    {\n        Draft      = 0,\n        Scheduled  = 1,\n        Published  = 2,\n        Archived   = 3,\n        Deleted    = 4\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>Represents an audit log entry for a <see cref=\"Post\" />.</summary>\n    public readonly record struct AuditLogEntry(DateTimeOffset AtUtc, string Description);\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Base contract for all domain events emitted by the core.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDomainEvent { }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Domain event emitted when a scheduled post is automatically\n    ///     published by the <see cref=\"PublishingAutomationService\" />.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record ScheduledPostPublishedEvent(\n        Guid PostId,\n        string Slug,\n        DateTimeOffset PublishedUtc) : IDomainEvent;\n\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    //  SHARED KERNEL & EXCEPTIONS\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Simple base entity with an ID and equality helper.\n    /// </summary>\n    public abstract class Entity<TId> : IEquatable<Entity<TId>>\n    {\n        public TId Id { get; init; } = default!;\n\n        public bool Equals(Entity<TId>? other)\n            => ReferenceEquals(this, other) || (other is not null && EqualityComparer<TId>.Default.Equals(Id, other.Id));\n\n        public override bool Equals(object? obj) => obj is Entity<TId> other && Equals(other);\n\n        public override int GetHashCode() => EqualityComparer<TId>.Default.GetHashCode(Id);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Thrown when an optimistic concurrency conflict occurs (e.g., stale\n    ///     version token).\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ConcurrencyException : Exception\n    {\n        public ConcurrencyException(string? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _logger         = logger          ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            // Resilience: three retries with exponential back-off\n            _retryPolicy = Policy\n                .Handle<Exception>()\n                .WaitAndRetryAsync(\n                    retryCount: 3,\n                    sleepDurationProvider: attempt => TimeSpan.FromSeconds(Math.Pow(2, attempt)),\n                    onRetry: (ex, ts, attempt, ctx) =>\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                            \"Retry {Attempt} while publishing scheduled posts. Waiting {Delay}.\",\n                            attempt, ts);\n                    });\n        }\n\n        /// <inheritdoc />\n        public async Task<int> PublishDuePostsAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Scheduled publishing job started at {StartTime}.\", _clock.UtcNow);\n\n            // Retrieve due posts\n            IReadOnlyCollection<Post> duePosts = await _postRepository\n                .FindScheduledDueAsync(_clock.UtcNow, ct)\n                .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (!duePosts.Any())\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"No scheduled posts due for publishing.\");\n                return 0;\n            }\n\n            int publishedCount = 0;\n\n            foreach (Post post in duePosts)\n            {\n                if (ct.IsCancellationRequested) break;\n\n                bool success = await PublishSingleAsync(post, ct)\n                    .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                if (success)\n                    publishedCount++;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"{Count} scheduled posts published.\", publishedCount);\n            return publishedCount;\n        }\n\n        private async Task<bool> PublishSingleAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            return await _retryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(async () =>\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    var validation = PublishingWindowValidator.Validate(post, _clock.UtcNow);\n\n                    if (!validation.IsValid)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(\n                            \"Skipping post {PostId} \u2013 publishing window invalid: {Reason}\",\n                            post.Id, validation.Reason);\n\n                        return false;\n                    }\n\n                    post.MarkAsPublished(_clock.UtcNow);\n\n                    await _unitOfWork.SaveChangesAsync(ct)\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    // Invalidate page caches\n                    await _cache.InvalidateAsync(CacheKeys.Post(post.Id), ct)\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    await _cache.InvalidateAsync(CacheKeys.HomePage, ct)\n                        .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                    // Pre-warm the post page to {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Error publishing post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                    throw; // Bubble up to Polly for retry\n                }\n            });\n        }\n PublishingWindowValidator\n    {\n        internal static PublishValidationResult Validate(Post post, DateTimeOffset nowUtc)\n        {\n            if (post == null)  return PublishValidationResult.Invalid(\"Post is null.\");\n\n            if (post.Status != PostStatus.Scheduled)\n                return PublishValidationResult.Invalid(\"Post status is not 'Scheduled'.\");\n\n            if (post.ScheduledPublishDate == null)\n                return PublishValidationResult.Invalid(\"Post does not have a scheduled date.\");\n\n            if (post.ScheduledPublishDate > nowUtc)\n                return PublishValidationResult.Invalid(\"Scheduled date is in the future.\");\n\n            return PublishValidationResult.Valid();\n        }\n } = PostStatus.Draft;\n        public DateTimeOffset? ScheduledPublishUtc { get; private set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishedUtc { get; private set; }\n\n        // EF-Core, Dapper, or serialization\n        private Post() { }\n\n        public Post(Guid id, string title, string slug)\n        {\n            Id   = id;\n            Title = title;\n            Slug  = slug;\n        }\n\n        public void Schedule(DateTimeOffset publishUtc)\n        {\n            if (Status != PostStatus.Draft)\n                throw new DomainException(\"Only draft posts can be scheduled.\");\n\n            ScheduledPublishUtc = publishUtc;\n            Status              = PostStatus.Scheduled;\n        }\n\n        public void Publish(IDateTimeProvider clock)\n        {\n            if (Status != PostStatus.Scheduled)\n                throw new DomainException(\"Only scheduled posts can be published.\");\n\n            if (clock.UtcNow < ScheduledPublishUtc)\n                throw new DomainException(\"Cannot publish before scheduled time.\");\n\n            PublishedUtc = clock.UtcNow;\n            Status }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Fired whenever a post becomes publicly available.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name=\"postId\">Identifier of the published post.</param>\n    /// <param private const int MaxBatchSize = 250; // Fail-fast boundary to protect downstream resources.\n\n        private readonly IPostRepository   _postRepository;\n        private readonly IEventBus         _eventBus;\n        private readonly IDateTimeProvider _clock;\n        private readonly IUnitOfWork       _uow;\n        private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> _logger;\n\n        public ScheduledPublishingService(\n            IPostRepository   postRepository,\n            IEventBus         eventBus,\n            IDateTimeProvider clock,\n            IUnitOfWork       uow,\n            ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> logger)\n        {\n            _postRepository = postRepository  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _eventBus       = eventBus        ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventBus));\n            _clock          = clock           ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _uow            = uow             ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(uow));\n            _logger         = logger          ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Publishes all posts whose scheduled timestamp is equal or earlier than the current time.\n        /// Uses a defensive batching approach to minimise contention and avoid OOM on massive queues.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<int> PublishDuePostsAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            var now = _clock.UtcNow;\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"ScheduledPublishingService scanning for publications due at {PublicationTime:u}\", now);\n\n            var candidates = await _postRepository.GetPostsPendingPublicationAsync(now, cancellationToken);\n\n            if (!candidates.Any())\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No posts to publish at {Moment:u}\", now);\n                return 0;\n            }\n\n            // We only take up to MaxBatchSize \u2013 additional items will be processed by the next run.\n            var batch = candidates\n                .OrderBy(p => p.ScheduledPublishUtc ?? DateTimeOffset.MinValue)\n                .Take(MaxBatchSize)\n                .ToArray();\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Discovered {Count} post(s) eligible for publication\", batch.Length);\n\n            foreach (var post in batch)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    post.Publish(_clock);\n                }\n                catch (DomainException dex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\n                        dex,\n                        \"Domain rules prevented publication of Post[{PostId}] \u2013 {@Post}\",\n                        post.Id,\n                        post);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(\n                        ex,\n                        \"Unexpected error while publishing Post[{PostId}] \u2013 Service will continue processing others\",\n                        post.Id);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Persist all mutated aggregates atomically.\n            await _postRepository.SaveAsync(batch, cancellationToken);\n\n            // Commit eventual cross-repository work.\n            await _uow.CommitAsync(cancellationToken);\n\n            // Dispatch domain events outside the transactional boundary.\n            foreach (var @event in batch.SelectMany(p => p.DomainEvents))\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    await _eventBus.PublishAsync(@event, cancellationToken);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(\n                        ex,\n                        \"Failed to publish event {@Event} for Post[{PostId}]\",\n                        @event,\n                        ( @event as PostPublishedEvent )?.PostId);\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Clear the events to avoid duplicate dispatching if the aggregate is rehydrated later.\n            foreach (var post in batch)\n                post.ClearDomainEvents();\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Publishing pipeline completed \u2013 {Count} post(s) processed\", batch.Length);\n\n            return batch.Length;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

All those\n//     concerns are funneled through abstract ports.\n//\n// --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Application.Publishing\n{\n    #region Domain & Port Abstractions\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Simplified aggregate root representing a blog post.\n    /// Only the properties required for scheduled publishing are included.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class Post\n    {\n        private readonly List<IDomainEvent> _domainEvents = new();\n\n        public Guid   Id          { get; private init; }\n        public string Title       { get; private set; } = string.Empty;\n        public string Slug        { get; private set; } = string.Empty;\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishAt  { get; private set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishedAt { get; private set; }\n        public PostStatus Status  { get; private set; }\n        public byte[] RowVersion  { get; private set; } = Array.Empty<byte>();\n\n        // Factory method for ORMs / mappers\n        private Post() { }\n\n        public Post(Guid id, string title, string slug, DateTimeOffset publishAt)\n        {\n            Id        = id;\n            Title     = title;\n            Slug      = slug;\n            PublishAt = publishAt;\n            Status    = PostStatus.Scheduled;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Transitions the aggregate to \u201cPublished\u201d and records domain events.\n        /// Validation is performed to guarantee aggregate invariants.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <exception cref=\"InvalidPostStateException\"/>\n        public void Publish(DateTimeOffset utcNow)\n        {\n            if (Status == PostStatus.Published)\n                throw new InvalidPostStateException(\"Post is already published.\");\n\n            if (Status != PostStatus.Scheduled)\n                throw new InvalidPostStateException($\"Cannot publish post in '{Status}' status.\");\n\n            if (PublishAt.HasValue && PublishAt.Value > utcNow)\n                throw new InvalidPostStateException(\"Cannot publish before the scheduled date.\");\n\n            PublishedAt = utcNow;\n            Status      = PostStatus.Published;\n\n            AddEvent(new PostPublishedEvent(Id, PublishedAt.Value));\n        }\n\n        public IReadOnlyCollection<IDomainEvent> CollectEvents()\n        {\n            var events = _domainEvents.AsReadOnly();\n            _domainEvents.Clear();\n            return events;\n        }\n\n        private void AddEvent(IDomainEvent @event) => _domainEvents.Add(@event);\n    }\n\n    public enum PostStatus\n    {\n        Draft      = 0,\n        Scheduled  = 1,\n        Published  = 2,\n        Archived   = 3\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Base marker interface for all domain events.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDomainEvent { }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Emitted after a post transitions from \u201cScheduled\u201d to \u201cPublished\u201d.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record PostPublishedEvent(Guid PostId, DateTimeOffset PublishedAt) : IDomainEvent;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Repository port for retrieving & persisting Post aggregates.\n    /// Implemented in the infrastructure layer (e.g. EF Core, Dapper, MongoDB).\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPostRepository\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Returns posts that should be published at or before <paramref name=\"utcThreshold\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task<IReadOnlyCollection<Post>> FindScheduledBeforeAsync(\n            DateTimeOffset utcThreshold,\n            int batchSize,\n            CancellationToken ct = default);\n\n        Task UpdateAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Port to wrap transaction boundaries so the publisher can treat persistence as atomic.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IUnitOfWork : IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        Task CommitAsync(CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Port for publishing domain events. Implementations can forward to MediatR,\n    /// an in-house event bus, or an external message queue (RabbitMQ, Kafka, etc.).\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDomainEventDispatcher\n    {\n        Task DispatchAsync(IDomainEvent @event, CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Port for time retrieval to keep the code deterministic and testable.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IClock\n    {\n        DateTimeOffset UtcNow { get; }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Exceptions\n\n    public sealed class InvalidPostStateException : Exception\n    {\n        public InvalidPostStateException(string message) : base(message) { }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Thrown when a scheduled publish attempt fails after max retries\n    /// so the error handler (Hangfire / Quartz) can bubble it up.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublishFailureException : Exception\n    {\n        public ScheduledPublishFailureException(string message, Exception? inner = null)\n            : base(message, inner) { }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Application Service\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Application service invoked by a background job scheduler (Hangfire, Quartz, Azure Function, etc.).\n    /// Scans for scheduled posts and publishes them in transactional batches.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublisher\n    {\n        private const int DefaultBatchSize = 250;\n        private const int MaxRetryAttempts = 3;\n\n        private readonly IPostRepository           _postRepo;\n        private readonly IUnitOfWork               _uow;\n        private readonly IDomainEventDispatcher    _dispatcher;\n        private readonly IClock                    _clock;\n        private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublisher> _logger;\n\n        public ScheduledPublisher(\n            IPostRepository postRepo,\n            IUnitOfWork uow,\n            IDomainEventDispatcher dispatcher,\n            IClock clock,\n            ILogger<ScheduledPublisher> logger)\n        {\n            _postRepo   = postRepo  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepo));\n            _uow        = uow       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(uow));\n            _dispatcher = dispatcher?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(dispatcher));\n            _clock      = clock     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _logger     = logger    ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Entry point executed by the scheduler.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task ExecuteAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"ScheduledPublisher started at {UtcNow}\", _clock.UtcNow);\n\n            DateTimeOffset threshold = _clock.UtcNow;\n\n            IReadOnlyCollection<Post> candidates;\n            try\n            {\n                candidates = await _postRepo.FindScheduledBeforeAsync(threshold, DefaultBatchSize, ct);\n            }\n            catch (Exception dbEx)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(dbEx, \"Failed to retrieve scheduled posts.\");\n                throw new ScheduledPublishFailureException(\"Database read failure.\", dbEx);\n            }\n\n            if (candidates.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"No posts eligible for publishing at this time.\");\n                return;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Found {Count} post(s) scheduled for publishing.\", candidates.Count);\n\n            foreach (var post in candidates)\n            {\n                // Publish each post in isolation so failure of one does not cancel the entire batch\n                bool success = await PublishWithRetriesAsync(post, ct);\n                if (!success)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\"Failed to publish post {PostId} after {MaxAttempts} attempts.\", post.Id, MaxRetryAttempts);\n                }\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"ScheduledPublisher finished at {UtcNow}\", _clock.UtcNow);\n        }\n\n        private async Task<bool> PublishWithRetriesAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            for (int attempt = 1; attempt <= MaxRetryAttempts; attempt++)\n            {\n                try\n                {\n                    await PublishPostAsync(post, ct);\n                    return true;\n                }\n                catch (InvalidPostStateException invalidEx)\n                {\n                    // Invariant violation \u2013 there is no point retrying\n                    _logger.LogWarning(invalidEx, \n                        \"Invariant violation while publishing post {PostId}. Skipping retry.\",\n                        post.Id);\n                    return false;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex) when (attempt < MaxRetryAttempts)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                        \"Attempt {Attempt} failed for post {PostId}. Retrying...\",\n                        attempt, post.Id);\n\n                    await Task.Delay(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(200 * attempt), ct);\n                }\n                catch (Exception finalEx)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(finalEx,\n                        \"Final attempt failed for post {PostId}. Giving up.\",\n                        post.Id);\n                    return false;\n                }\n            }\n\n            return false;\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Publishes a single post inside a transactional boundary.\n        /// </summary>\n        private async Task PublishPostAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Publishing post {PostId}\", post.Id);\n\n            post.Publish(_clock.UtcNow);\n\n            try\n            {\n                await _postRepo.UpdateAsync(post, ct);\n\n                // Persist aggregate & events in a single transaction\n                await _uow.CommitAsync(ct);\n\n                foreach (var domainEvent in post.CollectEvents())\n                {\n                    await _dispatcher.DispatchAsync(domainEvent, ct);\n                    _logger.LogDebug(\"Dispatched {EventType} for PostId={PostId}\", \n                        domainEvent.GetType().Name, post.Id);\n                }\n\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully published post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n            }\n            catch\n            {\n                // Let the caller decide to retry, but dispose/unit-of-work must roll back\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Rolling back transaction for post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

The code is production-ready, follows our hexagonal\n// design rules, and is safe to swap out (i.e. replace Quartz with Hangfire)\n// without touching the core domain.\n//\n// References (NuGet):\n//   - Quartz           (scheduler)\n//   - Microsoft.Extensions.Logging.Abstractions\n//   - TempoScribePro.Core (domain models & contracts)\n//\n// Author: TempoScribe Pro Team\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing Microsoft.Extensions.Logging;\nusing Quartz;\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Core.PublishingAutomation\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Port that defines how the core domain schedules a post\n    /// for future publication. IAsyncDisposable\n    {\n        private const string JobGroup   = \"TempoScribePro.PostPublishing\";\n        private const string TriggerGrp = \"TempoScribePro.PublishTriggers\";\n\n        private public async Task ScheduleAsync(ScheduledPost post, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            if (post == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(post));\n\n            ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n            var jobKey = CreateJobKey(post.Id);\n            if (await _scheduler.CheckExists(jobKey, ct))\n            {\n                // Replace existing schedule (idempotent behaviour)\n                await CancelAsync(post.Id, ct);\n            }\n\n            var job = JobBuilder\n                .Create<PublishPostJob>()\n                .WithIdentity(jobKey)\n                .UsingJobData(nameof(ScheduledPost.Id),        post.Id.ToString())\n                .UsingJobData(nameof(ScheduledPost.AuthorId),  post.AuthorId.ToString())\n                .UsingJobData(nameof(ScheduledPost.Title),     post.Title)\n                .Build();\n\n            var trigger = TriggerBuilder\n                .Create()\n                .WithIdentity(CreateTriggerKey(post.Id))\n                .StartAt(post.PublishAtUtc.UtcDateTime)\n                .WithSimpleSchedule(x => x.WithMisfireHandlingInstructionFireNow())\n                .ForJob(job)\n                .Build();\n\n            await _scheduler.ScheduleJob(job, trigger, ct);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Scheduled post '{Title}' (Id: {Id}) for {PublishAt}.\",\n CreateJobKey(postId);\n            var deleted = await _scheduler.DeleteJob(jobKey, ct);\n\n            if (deleted)\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Cancelled scheduled publication for PostId {PostId}.\", postId);\n            else\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"Attempted to cancel non-existent schedule for PostId {PostId}.\", postId);\n\n            return deleted;\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Quartz bookkeeping helpers\n\n        private static JobKey CreateJobKey(Guid postId) =>\n            new JobKey($\"PublishPost#{postId}\", JobGroup);\n\n public async ValueTask DisposeAsync()\n        {\n            if (!_scheduler.IsShutdown)\n            {\n                await _scheduler.Shutdown(waitForJobsToComplete: false);\n            }\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Quartz job that raises a domain event to publish a post.\n    /// In the real system the event would be dispatched to an application    }\n    }\n}\n```",

PublishedAt   { get; private set; }\n        private readonly List<IDomainEvent> _events = new();\n\n        // Domain factory.\n        public static Post Schedule(string title, string content, return new Post\n            {\n                Title       = title,\n                Content     = content,\n                ScheduledAt = scheduledAtUtc.UtcDateTime,\n                IsPremium   = isPremium,\n                Status      = PostStatus.Scheduled\n            };\n        }\n\n        public void Publish(IClock clock)\n        {\n            if (Status != PostStatus.Scheduled)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException($\"Cannot publish post in state {Status}\");\n            if (clock.UtcNow < ScheduledAt)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Cannot publish before scheduled date.\");\n\n            Status      = PostStatus.Published;\n            PublishedAt = clock.UtcNow;\n\n            _events.Add(new PostPublishedEvent(Id));\n        }\n\n        public void MarkFailed(string reason, IClock clock)\n        {\n            Status      = PostStatus.Failed;\n            PublishedAt = clock.UtcNow;\n            _events.Add(new PostPublishFailedEvent(Id, reason));\n        }\n\n        public IReadOnlyCollection<IDomainEvent> DequeueEvents()\n        {\n            var snapshot = _events.ToArray();\n            _events.Clear();\n            return snapshot;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Domain Events\n\n    public interface IDomainEvent { }\n\n    public sealed record PostPublishedEvent(PostId PostId)      : IDomainEvent;\n    public sealed record PostPublishFailedEvent(PostId PostId, string Reason) : IDomainEvent;\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Application Service\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Orchestrates scheduled publishing for posts that are due.\n    /// Intended to be executed by a hosted background worker or a serverless job.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublishingService\n    {\n        private const string CacheKeyPrefix     = \"scheduler:next:\";\n        private readonly IPostRepository        _repository;\n        private readonly IPaymentGateway        _paymentGateway;\n        private readonly ICacheAdapter          _cache;\n        private readonly IClock                 _clock;\n        private readonly IEventBus              _eventBus;\n        private readonly ILogger                _logger;\n        private readonly TimeSpan               _lookAhead;\n        private readonly SemaphoreSlim          _mutex            = new(1, 1);\n\n        public ScheduledPublishingService(\n            IPostRepository repository,\n            IPaymentGateway paymentGateway,\n            ICacheAdapter cache,\n            IClock clock,\n            IEventBus eventBus,\n            ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> logger,\n            TimeSpan? lookAheadWindow = null)\n        {\n            _repository     = repository  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(repository));\n            _paymentGateway = paymentGateway ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(paymentGateway));\n            _cache          = cache       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(cache));\n            _clock          = clock       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n            _lookAhead      = lookAheadWindow ?? TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Publishes every post that has reached its scheduled time.\n        /// Returns number of posts successfully published.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<int> PublishDuePostsAsync(CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            // Ensures single execution at a time even if the job is triggered in parallel.\n            if (!await _mutex.WaitAsync(TimeSpan.Zero, ct))\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Scheduler is already running \u2013 skipping concurrent execution.\");\n                return 0;\n            }\n\n            try\n            {\n                var now      = _clock.UtcNow;\n                var cacheKey = CacheKeyPrefix + now.UtcDateTime.ToString(\"yyyyMMddHHmm\");\n\n                // Attempt to pull scheduled posts from the cache first.\n                var duePosts = await _cache.GetAsync<IReadOnlyList<Post>>(cacheKey, ct)\n                               ?? await FetchAndCacheAsync(cacheKey, now, ct);\n\n                if (duePosts.Count == 0)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogTrace(\"No posts due for publication at {Time}.\", now);\n                    return 0;\n                }\n\n                int publishedCount = 0;\n                foreach (var post in duePosts.Where(p => p.Status == PostStatus.Scheduled))\n                {\n                    try\n                    {\n                        ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                        _logger.LogInformation(\n                            \"Publishing post {PostId} (Premium:{IsPremium}).\", post.Id, post.IsPremium);\n\n                        // Place premium post behind a pay wall first.\n                        if (post.IsPremium)\n                        {\n                            await _paymentGateway.EnsurePayWallAsync(post, ct);\n                            _logger.LogDebug(\"Paywall configured for post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                        }\n\n                        post.Publish(_clock);\n\n                        await _repository.SaveAsync(post, ct);\n                        await EmitEventsAsync(post, ct);\n\n                        publishedCount++;\n                    }\n                    catch (Exception ex)\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogError(ex,\n                            \"Error while publishing post {PostId}. Marking as failed.\", post.Id);\n\n                        post.MarkFailed(ex.Message, _clock);\n                        await _repository.SaveAsync(post, ct);\n                        await EmitEventsAsync(post, ct);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Scheduler successfully published {Count} posts.\", publishedCount);\n                return publishedCount;\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                _mutex.Release();\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task<IReadOnlyList<Post>> FetchAndCacheAsync(\n            string cacheKey,\n            DateTimeOffset now,\n            CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            // Look ahead to reduce DB hits for near-future runs.\n            var horizon = now + _lookAhead;\n            var posts   = await _repository.GetScheduledPostsAsync(horizon, ct);\n\n            // Cache for 30 seconds to keep things fresh but still reduce load.\n            await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, posts, TimeSpan.FromSeconds(30), ct);\n            return posts;\n        }\n\n        private async Task EmitEventsAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            foreach (var domainEvent in post.DequeueEvents())\n            {\n                await _eventBus.PublishAsync(domainEvent, ct);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Simple Adapters (In-Memory)\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Thread-safe, in-memory cache implementation suitable for unit tests and local dev.\n    /// Production deployments should replace it with Redis/Memcached adapter.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class InMemoryCacheAdapter : ICacheAdapter\n    {\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<string, CacheEntry> _store = new();\n\n        public Task<T?> GetAsync<T>(string key, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            if (_store.TryGetValue(key, out var entry) && !entry.IsExpired)\n                return Task.FromResult((T?)entry.Value);\n\n            _store.TryRemove(key, out _);\n            return Task.FromResult(default(T));\n        }\n\n        public Task SetAsync<T>(string key, T value, TimeSpan ttl, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            var expires = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow + ttl;\n            _store[key] = new CacheEntry(value!, expires);\n            return Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n\n        private sealed class CacheEntry\n        {\n            public object Value { get; }\n            private readonly DateTimeOffset _expiresAt;\n\n            public bool IsExpired => DateTimeOffset.UtcNow >= _expiresAt;\n\n            public CacheEntry(object value, DateTimeOffset expiresAt)\n            {\n                Value       = value;\n                _expiresAt  = expiresAt;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Na\u00efve payment gateway adapter used for local development.\n    /// In production this would integrate with Stripe/PayPal etc.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class MockPaymentGateway : IPaymentGateway\n    {\n        private readonly ILogger _logger;\n\n        public MockPaymentGateway(ILogger<MockPaymentGateway> logger) => _logger = logger;\n\n        public Task EnsurePayWallAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Mock paywall applied to post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n            return Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",
