payload = new DiffCachePayload(diffHtml);\n\n            await _cache.SetStringAsync(key, JsonConvert.SerializeObject(payload), _entryOptions, ct);\n            _logger.LogTrace(\"Cached diff for Post {PostId} (key={Key})\", postId, key);\n        }\n\n        public async Task<string?> TryGetAsync(Guid postId, DateTime draftUpdatedUtc, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            var key = BuildKey(postId, draftUpdatedUtc);\n            var json = await _cache.GetStringAsync(key, ct);\n\n            if (json == null)\n            {\n                return null;\n            }\n\n            try\n            {\n                var payload = JsonConvert.DeserializeObject<DiffCachePayload>(json);\n                return payload?.DiffHtml;\n            }\n            catch (JsonException ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Corrupted diff cache entry detected (key={Key}) \u2013 purging.\", key);\n                await _cache.RemoveAsync(key, ct);\n                return null;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static string BuildKey(Guid postId, DateTime updatedUtc)\n            => $\"livepreview:{postId:N}:{updatedUtc:yyyyMMddHHmmssffff}\";\n\n        private sealed record DiffCachePayload(string DiffHtml);\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Infrastructure \u2013 Simple Html Diff Generator\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// A basic diff generator that operates on Markdown input and highlights line-level changes.\n    /// Replace with a more sophisticated semantic diff (e.g. using diff-match-patch) as needed.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class SimpleHtmlDiffGenerator : IDiffGenerator\n    {\n        public Task<string> GenerateDiffHtmlAsync(string? oldMarkdown, string newMarkdown, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            // For demonstration, compute a na\u00efve line-by-line diff and wrap changes in <ins>/<del>.\n            var oldLines = (oldMarkdown ?? string.Empty).Split('\\n');\n            var newLines = newMarkdown.Split('\\n');\n\n            var diffBuilder = new StringBuilder();\n            var max = Math.Max(oldLines.Length, newLines.Length);\n\n            for (int i = 0; i < max; i++)\n            {\n                ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n                var oldLine = i < oldLines.Length ? oldLines[i] : null;\n                var newLine = i < newLines.Length ? newLines[i] : null;\n\n                if (oldLine == newLine)\n                {\n                    diffBuilder.AppendLine(System.Web.HttpUtility.HtmlEncode(newLine ?? string.Empty));\n                }\n                else\n                {\n                    if (oldLine is not null)\n                    {\n                        diffBuilder.Append(\"<del class=\\\"ts-diff-del\\\">\")\n                                   .Append(System.Web.HttpUtility.HtmlEncode(oldLine))\n                                   .AppendLine(\"</del>\");\n                    }\n\n                    if (newLine is not null)\n                    {\n                        diffBuilder.Append(\"<ins class=\\\"ts-diff-ins\\\">\")\n                                   .Append(System.Web.HttpUtility.HtmlEncode(newLine))\n                                   .AppendLine(\"</ins>\");\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            // Wrap in a container so styling can be applied by the front-end.\n            var html = $\"<div class=\\\"ts-diff\\\">{diffBuilder}</div>\";\n            return Task.FromResult(html);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Dependency Injection Extension\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Adds LivePreview services and their adapters to the .NET DI container.\n    /// </summary>\n    public static class LivePreviewServiceCollectionExtensions\n    {\n        public static IServiceCollection AddLivePreviewModule(this IServiceCollection services)\n        {\n            // Ports\n            services.AddTransient<ILivePreviewService, LivePreviewService>();\n\n            // Domain services\n            services.AddSingleton<IDiffGenerator, SimpleHtmlDiffGenerator>();\n\n            // Adapters\n            services.AddSingleton<IDiffCache, DistributedDiffCache>();\n\n            // Repositories (IPostReadRepository) should already be registered by the data access layer.\n\n            return services;\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <inheritdoc/>\n        public async Task<EditorialEfficiencyReport> GetEfficiencyReportAsync(\n            DateTime fromUtc,\n            DateTime toUtc,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            if (fromUtc > toUtc)\n            {\n                throw new ValidationException(\"'fromUtc' cannot be after 'toUtc'.\");\n            }\n\n            var cacheKey = BuildCacheKey(fromUtc, toUtc);\n\n            // 1. Try fast-path: return cached report if available.\n            if (await _cache.TryGetAsync<EditorialEfficiencyReport>(cacheKey, cancellationToken) is { } cached)\n            {\n                _logger.Trace($\"Cache hit for analytics report [{cacheKey}].\");\n                return cached;\n            }\n\n            // 2. Fallback: compute report by projecting events.\n            _logger.Info($\"Cache miss for analytics report [{cacheKey}] \u2013 recomputing.\");\n\n            var events = await _eventStream\n                .ReadAsync(fromUtc, toUtc, cancellationToken)\n                .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            var report = ComputeReport(events, fromUtc, toUtc);\n\n            // 3. Persist summary for historic querying (CQRS read-model).\n            await _repository.UpsertAsync(report, cancellationToken);\n\n            // 4. Cache for subsequent reads.\n            await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, report, DefaultCacheTtl, cancellationToken);\n\n            return report;\n        }\n\n        // --------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // Helper methods\n        // --------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n        private static string BuildCacheKey(DateTime fromUtc, DateTime toUtc) =>\n            $\"{CachePrefix}{fromUtc:yyyyMMddHHmmss}:{toUtc:yyyyMMddHHmmss}\";\n\n        private static EditorialEfficiencyReport ComputeReport(\n            IEnumerable<IEditorialEvent> events,\n            DateTime fromUtc,\n            DateTime toUtc)\n        {\n            // We rely on LINQ for in-memory projection because event counts per\n            // timeframe are modest (<100k). For larger volumes consider\n            // incremental snapshots or Map-Reduce.\n            var groupedByPost = events\n                .GroupBy(e => e.PostId)\n                .ToArray();\n\n            int totalPostsPublished = 0;\n            double avgDraftIterations = 0;\n            double avgTimeToPublishMinutes = 0;\n            int totalWordsProduced = 0;\n\n            foreach (var postEvents in groupedByPost)\n            {\n                var drafts = postEvents\n                    .Where(e => e is DraftUpdatedEvent)\n                    .Cast<DraftUpdatedEvent>()\n                    .OrderBy(e => e.UtcTimestamp)\n                    .ToList();\n\n                var published = postEvents\n                    .FirstOrDefault(e => e is PostPublishedEvent) as PostPublishedEvent;\n\n                if (published != null)\n                {\n                    totalPostsPublished++;\n\n                    if (drafts.Count > 0)\n                    {\n                        avgDraftIterations += drafts.Count;\n                        avgTimeToPublishMinutes +=\n                            (published.UtcTimestamp - drafts.First().UtcTimestamp).TotalMinutes;\n                    }\n\n                    totalWordsProduced += published.WordCount;\n                }\n            }\n\n            if (totalPostsPublished > 0)\n            {\n                avgDraftIterations /= totalPostsPublished;\n                avgTimeToPublishMinutes /= totalPostsPublished;\n            }\n\n            return new EditorialEfficiencyReport\n            (\n                ReportId: Guid.NewGuid(),\n                From: fromUtc,\n                To: toUtc,\n                TotalPostsPublished: totalPostsPublished,\n                AverageDraftIterations: Math.Round(avgDraftIterations, 2),\n                AverageMinutesToPublish: Math.Round(avgTimeToPublishMinutes, 2),\n                TotalWordsProduced: totalWordsProduced,\n                GeneratedAtUtc: DateTime.UtcNow\n            );\n        }\n    }\n}\n\n// ============================================================================\n// Domain contracts below. This is the per-preview expiration (minutes).\n        /// </summary>\n        public int LocalFallbackExpirationMinutes { get; init; } = 5;\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Amount of time (ms) allowed for distributed locks (SETNX) to be\n        /// acquired. If the lock cannot be acquired in this time window, the\n        /// operation is abandoned to keep latency low.\n        /// </summary>\n        public int LockWaitTimeoutMilliseconds { get; init; } = 200;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Domain-centric wrapped exception describing issues accessing or\n    /// manipulating preview cache entries.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ContentPreviewCacheException : Exception\n    {\n        public ContentPreviewCacheException(string message, Exception? inner = null)\n            : base(message, inner) { }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Ports / Hexagonal Interfaces\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Hexagonal port that allows domain services to store and retrieve live\n    /// preview snapshots of post drafts. Implementations may send calls to\n    /// Redis, Memcached, or any other storage.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IContentPreviewCache\n    {\n        /// <summary>Gets the latest preview snapshot HTML for a post, or null.</summary>\n        Task<string?> GetDraftPreviewAsync(Guid postId, CancellationToken ct = default);\n\n        /// <summary>Saves/updates the preview snapshot HTML for a post.</summary>\n        Task SaveDraftPreviewAsync(Guid postId, string html, CancellationToken ct = default);\n\n        /// <summary>Invalidates (removes) the cached preview for a post.</summary>\n        Task InvalidatePreviewAsync(Guid postId, CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Port responsible for generating human-readable differences between two\n    /// HTML strings. Falling back to in-memory cache.\");\n                if (_fallbackCache.TryGetValue<string>(key, out var fallback))\n                    return fallback;\n\n                throw new ContentPreviewCacheException(\n                    \"Failed to retrieve preview from Redis and fallback cache.\", ex);\n            }\n        }\n\n        public async Task SaveDraftPreviewAsync(Guid postId, string html, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            if (html is null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(html));\n            ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n            var key = BuildCacheKey(postId);\n            var lockKey = key + LockSuffix;\n            var lockValue = Environment.MachineName + \":\" + Guid.NewGuid().ToString(\"N\");\n\n            try\n            {\n                // Basic distributed lock using SET NX PX pattern\n                bool acquired = await _database.StringSetAsync(\n                    lockKey, lockValue,\n                    TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(_options.LockWaitTimeoutMilliseconds),\n                    When.NotExists);\n\n                if (!acquired)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogDebug(\"Lock acquisition timed out for PostId={PostId}\", postId);\n                    return; // Another write in progress; skip to avoid thrashing\n                }\n\n                await _database.StringSetAsync(\n                    key,\n                    html,\n                    TimeSpan.FromMinutes(_options.PreviewExpirationMinutes));\n\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Preview saved for PostId={PostId}\", postId);\n\n                _fallbackCache.Set(key, html,\n                    TimeSpan.FromMinutes(_options.LocalFallbackExpirationMinutes));\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Unable to save preview to Redis. Storing to fallback cache.\");\n                _fallbackCache.Set(key, html,\n                    TimeSpan.FromMinutes(_options.LocalFallbackExpirationMinutes));\n                throw new ContentPreviewCacheException(\"Failed to save preview to Redis.\", ex);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                // Best-effort lock release\n                try\n                {\n                    var currentValue = await _database.StringGetAsync(lockKey);\n                    if (currentValue == lockValue)\n                        await _database.KeyDeleteAsync(lockKey);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogDebug(ex, \"Error while releasing Redis lock for PostId={PostId}\", postId);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        public async Task InvalidatePreviewAsync(Guid postId, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            ct.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n            var key = BuildCacheKey(postId);\n            try\n            {\n                await _database.KeyDeleteAsync(key);\n                _fallbackCache.Remove(key);\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Preview invalidated for PostId={PostId}\", postId);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Unable to invalidate preview for PostId={PostId} in Redis.\", postId);\n                _fallbackCache.Remove(key); // Even if Redis fails, ensure local is cleared\n                throw new ContentPreviewCacheException(\"Failed to invalidate preview.\", ex);\n            }\n        }\n\n        private string BuildCacheKey(Guid postId)\n            => $\"{_options.KeyPrefix}{PreviewSuffix}|{postId.ToString(\"N\", CultureInfo.InvariantCulture)}\";\n\n        #region Dispose Pattern\n\n        private bool _disposed;\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            if (_disposed) return;\n\n            _fallbackCache?.Dispose();\n            _connection?.Dispose();\n\n            _disposed = true;\n            GC.SuppressFinalize(this);\n        }\n\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Diff Service Implementation\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Lightweight diffing implementation designed for HTML previews. The goal\n    /// is not a pixel-perfect diff, but a performant, readable markup (<ins>,\n    /// <del>) that editors can consume immediately in the live preview panel.\n    /// This implementation is intentionally simple to keep the dependency\n    /// footprint small; however, it can be transparently swapped for a more\n    /// advanced algorithm via the IPreviewDiffService port.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class HtmlPreviewDiffService : IPreviewDiffService\n    {\n        private readonly ILogger<HtmlPreviewDiffService> _logger;\n\n        public HtmlPreviewDiffService(ILogger<HtmlPreviewDiffService> logger)\n        {\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        public string ComputeDiff(string oldHtml, string newHtml)\n        {\n            if (oldHtml == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(oldHtml));\n            if (newHtml == null) throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(newHtml));\n\n            if (oldHtml.Equals(newHtml, StringComparison.Ordinal))\n                return newHtml; // No changes; return as-is to save cycles\n\n            try\n            {\n                var sb = new StringBuilder(EstimateCapacity(oldHtml, newHtml));\n\n                int i = 0, j = 0;\n                while (i < oldHtml.Length && j < newHtml.Length)\n                {\n                    if (oldHtml[i] == newHtml[j])\n                    {\n                        sb.Append(oldHtml[i]);\n                        i++; j++;\n                    }\n                    else\n                    {\n                        // Naive diff: mark deletions then insertions\n                        int startOld = i;\n                        int startNew = j;\n                        while (i < oldHtml.Length && (j >= newHtml.Length || oldHtml[i] != newHtml[j]))\n                            i++;\n\n                        while (j < newHtml.Length && (i >= oldHtml.Length || oldHtml[i] != newHtml[j]))\n                            j++;\n\n                        var deleted = oldHtml.Substring(startOld, i - startOld);\n                        var inserted = newHtml.Substring(startNew, j - startNew);\n\n                        if (deleted.Length > 0)\n                            sb.Append($\"<del>{System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(deleted)}</del>\");\n                        if (inserted.Length > 0)\n                            sb.Append($\"<ins>{System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(inserted)}</ins>\");\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (i < oldHtml.Length)\n                    sb.Append($\"<del>{System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(oldHtml.Substring(i))}</del>\");\n                if (j < newHtml.Length)\n                    sb.Append($\"<ins>{System.Net.WebUtility.HtmlEncode(newHtml.Substring(j))}</ins>\");\n\n                return sb.ToString();\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Diff generation failed. Falling back to newHtml.\");\n                return newHtml;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static int EstimateCapacity(string s1, string s2)\n            => (s1.Length + s2.Length) * 2; // Rough estimate for StringBuilder size\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

 Quartz cannot be reached (e.g., in unit tests or disconnected execution).\n//\n// NuGet dependencies (declared in csproj elsewhere):\n//     - Quartz (>= 3.4.0)\n//     - /// <summary>\n        /// Cancels a previously scheduled publication (if any).\n        /// </summary>\n        Task CancelScheduledPostAsync(PostId postId, CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Quartz Adapter\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Quartz\u2010powered implementation of <see cref=\"IPublishScheduler\"/>.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class   {\n            _publishCommand = publishCommand \n                              ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(publishCommand));\n            _logger         = logger \n                              ?? Scheduling retry.\", postId);\n                throw;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Fallback/In-Memory Adapter\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Minimal in\u2010memory scheduling implementation intended for unit tests or\n    /// single\u2010process execution environments where Quartz is unavailable.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class InMemoryPublishScheduler : IPublishScheduler, IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly ConcurrentDictionary<PostId, Timer> _timers  = new();\n        private readonly IPublishCommand                     _command;\n        private readonly ILogger<InMemoryPublishScheduler>    _logger;\n\n        public InMemoryPublishScheduler(\n            IPublishCommand command,\n            ILogger<InMemoryPublishScheduler>? logger = null)\n        {\n            _command = command \n                       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(command));\n            _logger  = logger \n                       ?? Microsoft.Extensions.Logging.Abstractions.NullLogger<InMemoryPublishScheduler>.Instance;\n        }\n\n        public Task SchedulePostAsync(PostId postId, DateTime utcPublishAt, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            if (utcPublishAt.Kind != DateTimeKind.Utc)\n                throw new ArgumentException(\"utcPublishAt must be expressed in UTC.\", nameof(utcPublishAt));\n\n            // Dispose previous timer if we are rescheduling.\n            if (_timers.TryRemove(postId, out var existing))\n                existing.Dispose();\n\n            var delay = utcPublishAt - DateTime.UtcNow;\n            if (delay < TimeSpan.Zero)\n                delay = TimeSpan.Zero; // Fire ASAP if in the past.\n\n            var timer = new Timer(async _ => await ExecutePublishAsync(postId),\n                                  null,\n                                  delay,\n                                  Timeout.InfiniteTimeSpan);\n\n            _timers[postId] = timer;\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"In-memory scheduled post {PostId} at {PublishAt:o}.\", postId, utcPublishAt);\n\n            return Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n\n        public Task CancelScheduledPostAsync(PostId postId, CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            if (_timers.TryRemove(postId, out var timer))\n            {\n                timer.Dispose();\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Cancelled in-memory scheduled post {PostId}.\", postId);\n            }\n\n            return Task.CompletedTask;\n        }\n\n        private async Task ExecutePublishAsync(PostId postId)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                await _command.PublishAsync(postId);\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"In-memory executed publication for post {PostId}.\", postId);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"In-memory publication failed for post {PostId}.\", postId);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                // Clean up timer to prevent memory leaks.\n                CancelScheduledPostAsync(postId).GetAwaiter().GetResult();\n            }\n        }\n\n        public void Dispose()\n        {\n            foreach (var kvp in _timers)\n                kvp.Value.Dispose();\n            _timers.Clear();\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Internal Commands\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Application service (or domain use\u2010case) responsible for publishing a post\n    /// immediately.  Abstraction allows the scheduler to stay isolated.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPublishCommand\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Executes an immediate publish operation, regardless of current status.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task PublishAsync(PostId postId, CancellationToken ct = default);\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

All rights reserved.\n// </copyright>\n// <summary>\n//   Production-grade implementation of the scheduled-publishing automation service.\n//   This service scans for posts whose PublishAt date is due and transitions them\n//   from \u201cScheduled\u201d to \u201cPublished\u201d, making sure that:\n//      \u2022 Concurrency is respected through a distributed lock\n//      \u2022 Domain events are emitted\n//      \u2022 All outward-facing concerns (cache invalidation, analytics, etc.) are\n//        handled via ports & adapters\n//\n//   Architectural notes\n//   -------------------\n//   The service sits in the Application layer (Service Layer pattern) and only\n//   depends on domain abstractions (repositories, ports).  All technology-specific\n//   implementations live inside adapters that the DI container wires up at runtime.\n//\n//   File path: src/module_55.txt\n//   Project  : TempoScribe Pro \u2013 Hexagonal Productivity Blog Suite\n//   Language : C# 10\n// --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n#nullable enable\n\nusing System;\nusing System.Collections.Generic;\nusing System.Threading;\nusing System.Threading.Tasks;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Domain.Posts;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Domain.Shared;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Ports.Cache;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Ports.Events;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Ports.Locking;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Ports.Logging;\nusing TempoScribePro.Core.Ports.Repositories;\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Core.Services.Automation;\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Orchestrates scheduled publishing of blog posts.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed class ScheduledPublishingService : IScheduledPublishingService\n{\n    private const string DistributedLockKey = \"tempo:scheduled-publishing:lock\";\n    private static readonly TimeSpan LockTtl = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(2);\n\n    private readonly IPostRepository            _postRepository;\n    private readonly IUnitOfWork                _unitOfWork;\n    private readonly IDateTimeProvider          _dateTimeProvider;\n    private readonly IEventDispatcher           _eventDispatcher;\n    private readonly IContentCache              _contentCache;\n    private readonly IDistributedLockProvider   _lockProvider;\n    private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> _logger;\n\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Ctor. All dependencies are injected by the IoC container.\n    /// </summary>\n    public ScheduledPublishingService(\n        IPostRepository                         postRepository,\n        IUnitOfWork                             unitOfWork,\n        IDateTimeProvider                       dateTimeProvider,\n        IEventDispatcher                        eventDispatcher,\n        IContentCache                           contentCache,\n        IDistributedLockProvider                lockProvider,\n        ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService>     logger)\n    {\n        _postRepository   = postRepository   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n        _unitOfWork       = unitOfWork       ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(unitOfWork));\n        _dateTimeProvider = dateTimeProvider ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(dateTimeProvider));\n        _eventDispatcher  = eventDispatcher  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventDispatcher));\n        _contentCache     = contentCache     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(contentCache));\n        _lockProvider     = lockProvider     ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(lockProvider));\n        _logger           = logger           ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n    }\n\n    /// <inheritdoc />\n    public async Task<int> PublishDueContentAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n    {\n        // Attempt to acquire a short-lived distributed lock to avoid duplicate work in scaled setups.\n        await using var distLock = await _lockProvider.TryAcquireAsync(\n                                        DistributedLockKey,\n                                        LockTtl,\n                                        cancellationToken);\n\n        if (!distLock.IsAcquired)\n        {\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"ScheduledPublishingService skipped execution because another node holds the lock.\");\n            return 0;\n        }\n\n        var now = _dateTimeProvider.UtcNow;\n        IReadOnlyCollection<Post> duePosts = await _postRepository\n            .GetDueScheduledPostsAsync(now, cancellationToken);\n\n        if (duePosts.Count == 0)\n        {\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"No posts were due for publishing at {Timestamp}\", now);\n            return 0;\n        }\n\n        _logger.LogInformation(\"Found {PostCount} post(s) due for publishing.\", duePosts.Count);\n\n        var publishedCount = 0;\n\n        foreach (var post in duePosts)\n        {\n            cancellationToken.ThrowIfCancellationRequested();\n\n            try\n            {\n                if (!post.CanTransitionToPublished())\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\n                        \"Post {PostId} is marked as scheduled but cannot transition to 'Published'. Skipping.\",\n                        post.Id);\n                    continue;\n                }\n\n                post.Publish(now);\n\n                publishedCount++;\n\n                // Persist the domain-state transition.\n                await _postRepository.UpdateAsync(post, cancellationToken);\n\n                // Dispatch domain events (e.g., PostPublishedEvent).\n                await _eventDispatcher.DispatchAsync(post.DomainEvents, cancellationToken);\n\n                // Bust cache entries eagerly to ensure readers see fresh content.\n                _contentCache.RemovePost(post.Id);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(\n                    ex,\n                    \"Failed to publish scheduled post {PostId}. Error: {Message}\",\n                    post.Id,\n                    ex.Message);\n                // Continue processing remaining posts without bubbling up.\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Commit once for all processed posts to minimize transaction overhead.\n        try\n        {\n            await _unitOfWork.CommitAsync(cancellationToken);\n        }\n        catch (Exception ex)\n        {\n            _logger.LogCritical(\n                ex,\n                \"UnitOfWork commit failed after publishing {Count} post(s). Rolling back.\",\n                publishedCount);\n\n            await _unitOfWork.RollbackAsync(cancellationToken);\n            throw; // Let higher-level handlers decide what to do.\n        }\n\n        _logger.LogInformation(\"ScheduledPublishingService published {Count} post(s).\", publishedCount);\n\n        return publishedCount;\n    }\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n///     Service-layer abstraction for scheduled publishing so that\n///     orchestrators (e.g., cron jobs, background workers) can trigger it\n///     without knowing implementation details.\n/// </summary>\npublic interface IScheduledPublishingService\n{\n    /// <summary>\n    ///     Publishes all posts whose <c>PublishAt</c> date is due.\n    /// </summary>\n    /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Optional cancellation token.</param>\n    /// <returns>Number of posts successfully published.</returns>\n    Task<int> PublishDueContentAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default);\n}\n```",

}\n\n        /// <inheritdoc/>\n        public async Task<PremiumPurchaseResult> PurchasePremiumPostAsync(\n            PremiumPurchaseRequest request,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(request);\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Initiating premium-post purchase {@Request}\", request);\n\n            var cacheKey = GetCacheKey(request.UserId, request.PostId);\n\n            // Fast-path: user already owns it, cached.\n            if (_cache.TryGetValue(cacheKey, out bool alreadyOwned) && alreadyOwned)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"User {UserId} already owns Post {PostId} (cache hit).\",\n                                 request.UserId, request.PostId);\n                return new PremiumPurchaseResult(\n                    Success: true,\n                    Message: \"Already purchased.\",\n                    ReceiptUrl: null,\n                    AlreadyOwned: true);\n            }\n\n            // Load post details.\n            var post = await _postRepo.FindByIdAsync(request.PostId, ct)\n                        ?? throw new PostNotFoundException(request.PostId);\n\n providerResult.FailureReason);\n                throw new PaymentFailedException(providerResult.FailureReason ?? \"Unknown failure\");\n            }\n\n            // Record purchase.\n post.Currency,\n                PurchasedAtUtc = _clock.UtcNow,\n                ProviderTransactionId = providerResult.ProviderTransactionId ?? string.Empty,\n                ReceiptUrl = token = default);\n    }\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Domain DTOs / Value Objects (Trimmed)\n    // In the real codebase these live inside the Core Domain project.\n    // Here we replicate minimal structure for compilation purposes.\n    public record PostMonetizationInfo(Guid PostId, bool IsPremium, decimal Price);\n    public record PaymentResult(bool Succeeded, string TransactionId, string? Error);\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Exceptions\n    /// <summary>Represents unrecoverable domain rule violations.</summary>\n    public sealed class DomainException : Exception\n    {\n        public DomainException(string message) : base(message) { }\n    }\n    #endregion\n\n    // =========================================================================\n    // Implementation\n    // =========================================================================\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Concrete implementation of <see cref=\"IPremiumAccessService\"/>.\n    /// Focuses exclusively on workflow orchestration; no framework-specific\n    /// code lives here.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class PremiumAccessService : IPremiumAccessService\n    {\n        private const string CacheKeyTemplate = \"premium_access:{0}:{1}\";\n        private static readonly TimeSpan CacheTtl = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(15);\n\n        private readonly IPaymentGateway _paymentGateway;\n        private readonly IPremiumAccessRepository _accessRepository;\n        private readonly IPostRepository _postRepository;\n        private readonly ICacheProvider _cache;\n        private readonly ILogger<PremiumAccessService> _logger;\n        private readonly AsyncRetryPolicy<PaymentResult> _paymentRetryPolicy;\n\n        public PremiumAccessService(\n            IPaymentGateway paymentGateway,\n            IPremiumAccessRepository accessRepository,\n            IPostRepository postRepository,\n            ICacheProvider cache,\n            ILogger<PremiumAccessService> logger)\n        {\n            _paymentGateway = paymentGateway ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(paymentGateway));\n            _accessRepository = accessRepository ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(accessRepository));\n            _postRepository = postRepository ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _cache = cache ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(cache));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            // Resilient retry: 2 retries with exponential back-off on transient failures\n            _paymentRetryPolicy = Policy<PaymentResult>\n                .Handle<Exception>() // network, 5xx, timeouts \u2026\n                .OrResult(r => !r.Succeeded)\n                .WaitAndRetryAsync(\n                    retryCount: 2,\n                    sleepDurationProvider: attempt => TimeSpan.FromSeconds(Math.Pow(2, attempt)),\n                    onRetry: (result, span, attempt, ctx) =>\n                    {\n                        if (result.Exception != null)\n                        {\n                            _logger.LogWarning(\n                                result.Exception,\n                                \"Payment attempt {Attempt} failed due to exception. Retrying in {Delay}\u2026\",\n                                attempt,\n                                span);\n                        }\n                        else\n                        {\n                            _logger.LogWarning(\n                                \"Payment attempt {Attempt} returned unsuccessful result. Retrying in {Delay}\u2026\",\n                                attempt,\n                                span);\n                        }\n                    });\n        }\n\n        /// <inheritdoc />\n        public async Task<bool> EnsureAccessAsync(Guid postId, Guid userId, CancellationToken token = default)\n        {\n            if (postId == Guid.Empty) throw new ArgumentException(\"PostId cannot be empty.\", nameof(postId));\n            if (userId == Guid.Empty) throw new ArgumentException(\"UserId cannot be empty.\", nameof(userId));\n\n            var cacheKey = string.Format(CacheKeyTemplate, postId, userId);\n\n            // 1. Short-circuit via cache\n            bool? cached = await _cache.GetAsync<bool?>(cacheKey, token);\n            if (cached.HasValue && cached.Value)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Cache hit for premium access ({PostId}, {UserId})\", postId, userId);\n                return true;\n            }\n\n            // 2. Consult repository as source of truth\n            if (await _accessRepository.HasAccessAsync(userId, postId, token))\n            {\n                await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, true, CacheTtl, token);\n                return true;\n            }\n\n            // 3. Retrieve post monetization info\n            PostMonetizationInfo info =\n                await _postRepository.GetMonetizationInfoAsync(postId, token)\n                    ?? throw new DomainException($\"Post {postId} not found.\");\n\n            if (!info.IsPremium)\n            {\n                // Free content \u21d2 Grant & cache\n                await _accessRepository.GrantAccessAsync(userId, postId, token);\n                await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, true, CacheTtl, token);\n                return true;\n            }\n\n            // 4. Attempt to charge\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Charging user {UserId} {Price:C} for post {PostId}\", userId, info.Price, postId);\n\n            PaymentResult payment = await _paymentRetryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(\n                async ct => await _paymentGateway.ChargeAsync(userId, postId, info.Price, ct),\n                token);\n\n            if (!payment.Succeeded)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(\n                    \"Payment failed for user {UserId} accessing post {PostId}. Reason: {Error}\",\n                    userId,\n                    postId,\n                    payment.Error ?? \"Unknown\");\n                return false;\n            }\n\n            // 5. Persist access grant post-payment\n            await _accessRepository.GrantAccessAsync(userId, postId, token);\n            await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, true, CacheTtl, token);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Premium access granted. TransactionId={TransactionId}\",\n                payment.TransactionId);\n\n            return true;\n        }\n    }\n}\n```",

new PostPublishedEvent(post.Id, utcNow);\n            await _eventBus.PublishAsync(evt, ct)\n                           .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"[Scheduler] Post _clock.UtcNow);\n            await _eventBus.PublishAsync(evt, ct)\n                           .ConfigureAwait(false);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region DTOs / Results how to act; plan retrieval is non-critical.\n            }\n        }\n        #endregion\n\n        #region Private helpers\n\n        private async Task<Customer> CreateOrGetCustomerAsync(string CustomerCreateOptions\n            {\n                Email = email\n            }, null, token);\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Created new Stripe customer {CustomerId} for {Email}.\", ParseMetadata(string? metadataJson)\n        {\n            if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(metadataJson))\n                return null;\n\n            try\n            {\n                return JsonSerializer.Deserialize<Dictionary<string, string>>(metadataJson);\n            }\n            catch\n            {\n                // Ignore malformed metadata to avoid blocking payment\n                return null;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static bool IsTransientStripeError(StripeException ex)\n        {\n            // 5xx or rate limiting are considered transient\n            return ex.StripeError?.Type == \"api_error\"\n                   || ex.HttpStatusCode is >= HttpStatusCode.InternalServerError\n                   || ex.StripeError?.Code == \"rate_limit\";\n        }\n\n        private static PaymentError MapStripeError(Exception ex)\n        {\n            return ex switch\n            {\n                StripeException stripeEx => new PaymentError(\n                    Code       : stripeEx.StripeError?.Code ?? stripeEx.Code.ToString(),\n                    Message    : stripeEx.StripeError?.Message ?? stripeEx.Message,\n                    HttpStatus : stripeEx.HttpStatusCode),\n                _ => new PaymentError(\n                    Code       : \"unknown_error\",\n                    Message    : ex.Message,\n                    HttpStatus : null)\n            };\n        }\n        #endregion\n    }\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

Build a new transaction aggregate.\n            var transaction = new PaymentTransaction(userId, targetId, amount, provider);\n\n            // 2. Persist initial state (pending).\n            await _transactionRepository.AddAsync(transaction, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // 3. Request authorization from chosen gateway.\n            var authResponse = await _paymentGateway.AuthorizeAsync(transaction, cancellationToken)\n                                                     .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (!authResponse.IsAuthorized)\n            {\n                // Authorization failed \u2014 mark and publish domain events.\n                transaction.MarkFailed($\"Authorization declined: {authResponse.DeclineReason}\");\n                await PersistAndPublishAsync(transaction, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                return new PaymentResult(\n                    transaction,\n                    IsSuccessful: false,\n                    ProviderReference: authResponse.ProviderReference,\n                    Metadata: new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"auth_decline_reason\"] = authResponse.DeclineReason ?? \"unknown\"\n                    },\n                    FailureReason: authResponse.DeclineReason);\n            }\n\n            // 4. Update transaction as authorized.\n            transaction.MarkAuthorized(authResponse.ProviderReference);\n            await _transactionRepository.UpdateAsync(transaction, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // 5. Attempt capture / settlement.\n            var settleResponse = await _paymentGateway.CaptureAsync(\n                transaction,\n                authResponse.ProviderReference,\n                cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            if (!settleResponse.IsSettled)\n            {\n                // Settlement failed \u2014 we keep transaction in Authorized state for potential retry.\n                await _domainEventPublisher.PublishAsync(transaction.DomainEvents, cancellationToken)\n                                            .ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n                return new PaymentResult(\n                    transaction,\n                    IsSuccessful: false,\n                    ProviderReference: settleResponse.ProviderReference,\n                    Metadata: new Dictionary<string, string>\n                    {\n                        [\"capture_failure_reason\"] = settleResponse.FailureReason ?? \"unknown\"\n                    },\n                    FailureReason: settleResponse.FailureReason);\n            }\n\n            // 6. Mark settled and persist final state.\n            transaction.MarkSettled(settleResponse.ProviderReference);\n            await PersistAndPublishAsync(transaction, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            return new PaymentResult(\n                transaction,\n                IsSuccessful: true,\n                ProviderReference: settleResponse.ProviderReference,\n                Metadata: null);\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Attempts to capture a previously authorized payment.\n        /// </summary>\n        public async Task<PaymentResult> CaptureAsync(\n            Guid transactionId,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            var transaction = await _transactionRepository.GetByIdAsync(transactionId, cancellationToken)\n                                                          .ConfigureAwait(false)\n                ??          _distributedLock = distributedLock ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(distributedLock));\n            _logger          = logger          ?? throw new cluster.\n            await using var lockHandle = await _distributedLock.TryAcquireAsync(\n                DistributedLockKey,\n                ttl: TimeSpan.FromMinutes(5),\n                cancellationToken);\n\n            if (lockHandle is null)\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Another node already owns the scheduled-publish lock.\");\n                return DO NOT await inside loop to avoid head-of-line blocking.\n                    _ = _eventDispatcher.PublishAsync(\n                        new PostPublishedEvent(post.Id, executionTimestampUtc),\n                        CancellationToken.None);\n\n                    publishResult.PublishedCount++;\n                }\n                catch (DomainValidationException dvx)\n                {\n                    // Domain error \u2013 mark the post as failed but continue processing.\n                    await MarkPostAsFailedAsync(post, dvx, cancellationToken);\n                    publishResult.FailedPostIds.Add(post.Id);\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogError(ex, \"Unexpected error while publishing post {PostId}\", post.Id);\n                    await MarkPostAsFailedAsync(post, ex, cancellationToken);\n                    publishResult.FailedPostIds.Add(post.Id);\n                }\n            }\n\n            publishResult.ExecutionTime = perf.Elapsed;\n            _logger.LogInformation(\n                \"Scheduled publish cycle finished in {Elapsed:g}. \" +\n                \"Published: {Published}. Failed: {Failed}.\",\n                publishResult.ExecutionTime,\n                publishResult.PublishedCount,\n                publishResult.FailedPostIds.Count);\n\n            return publishResult;\n        }\n\n        private async Task MarkPostAsFailedAsync(Post post, Exception ex, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            // We pessimistically set status to failed so that manual review is required.\n            post.GetType().GetProperty(\"Status\")!\n                .SetValue(post, PostStatus.PublicationFailed);\n\n            await _postRepository.UpdateAsync(post, ct);\n            _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                \"Post {PostId} marked as PublicationFailed due to an error.\",\n                post.Id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n\n    #region Utility\n\n    internal static class CacheKeys\n    {\n        public static string ForPost(PostId id) => $\"post:{id}\";\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Simple disposable that measures elapsed time of a code block.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class ExecutionTimer : IDisposable\n    {\n        private readonly DateTime _started = DateTime.UtcNow;\n        public  TimeSpan  Elapsed => DateTime.UtcNow - _started;\n        public void Dispose() { /* no op \u2013 just syntactic sugar */ }\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

The coordinator is intended\n    /// to be triggered by an adapter (e.g. Hangfire, Quartz.NET, AWS EventBridge,\n    /// or a simple Cron job) on a configurable interval.  It is implementation-\n    /// agnostic and safe to execute concurrently because post-state transitions\n    /// are guarded by pessimistic or optimistic locking in lower tiers.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublishingCoordinator\n    {\n        private const int DefaultBatchSize = 50;\n\n        private readonly IPostRepository      _postRepository;\n        private readonly IDomainEventDispatcher _eventDispatcher;\n        private readonly IUnitOfWork          _unitOfWork;\n        private readonly IDateTimeProvider    _clock;\n        private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublishingCoordinator> _logger;\n\n        public ScheduledPublishingCoordinator(\n            IPostRepository                   postRepository,\n            IDomainEventDispatcher            eventDispatcher,\n            IUnitOfWork                       unitOfWork,\n            IDateTimeProvider                 clock,\n            ILogger<ScheduledPublishingCoordinator> logger)\n        {\n            _postRepository  = postRepository  ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _eventDispatcher = eventDispatcher ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(eventDispatcher));\n            _unitOfWork      = unitOfWork      ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(unitOfWork));\n            _clock           = clock           ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _logger          = logger          ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Scans, publishes, and summarizes all posts that are ready for automatic\n        /// publication. irrecoverable persistence errors occur.\n        /// </exception>\n        public async Task<ScheduledPublishingSummary> ProcessPendingScheduledPostsAsync(\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken = default,\n            int batchSize = DefaultBatchSize)\n        {\n            var stopwatch = ValueStopwatch.StartNew();\n            int succeeded = 0;\n            int failed    = 0;\n            int inspected = 0;\n\n            try\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Scheduled-publishing routine started at {Now}.\", _clock.UtcNow);\n\n                List<Post> duePosts;\n                do\n                {\n                    duePosts = (await _postRepository\n                                    .GetScheduledPostsDueAsync(_clock.UtcNow, batchSize, cancellationToken))\n                                .ToList();\n\n                    inspected += duePosts.Count;\n\n                    foreach (var post in duePosts)\n                    {\n                        try\n                        {\n                            // Domain logic is encapsulated by the entity itself.\n                            post.Publish(_clock.UtcNow);\n\n                            // Persist immediately to release any database-level locks early.\n                            await _postRepository.UpdateAsync(post, cancellationToken);\n                            await _eventDispatcher.DispatchAndClearEventsAsync(post, cancellationToken);\n\n                            succeeded++;\n                            _logger.LogInformation(\n                                \"Post {PostId} ('{Title}') published successfully.\", post.Id, post.Title);\n                        }\n                        catch (PostDomainException ex)\n                        {\n                            failed++;\n                            _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                                \"Domain-level validation failed while publishing post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                        }\n                        catch (Exception ex)\n                        {\n                            failed++;\n                            _logger.LogError(ex,\n                                \"Unexpected error while publishing post {PostId}.\", post.Id);\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    // Commit after each batch to keep transactions lean and release locks quickly.\n                    if (duePosts.Any())\n                    {\n                        await _unitOfWork.CommitAsync(cancellationToken);\n                    }\n\n                } while (duePosts.Count == batchSize && !cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested);\n\n                var summary = new ScheduledPublishingSummary(\n                    inspectedPosts: inspected,\n                    publishedPosts: succeeded,\n                    failedPosts: failed,\n                    elapsed: stopwatch.Elapsed);\n\n                _logger.LogInformation(\n                    \"Scheduled-publishing routine completed in {ElapsedSeconds:n1}s. \" +\n                    \"{Published}/{Total} posts published; {Failed} failed.\",\n                    summary.Elapsed.TotalSeconds,\n                    summary.PublishedPosts,\n                    summary.InspectedPosts,\n                    summary.FailedPosts);\n\n                return summary;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when (!(ex is ScheduledPublishingException))\n            {\n                _logger.LogCritical(ex,\n                    \"Fatal error occurred in scheduled-publishing coordinator. \" +\n                    \"Execution aborted; manual intervention may be required.\");\n\n                throw new ScheduledPublishingException(\n                    \"An unexpected error occurred while processing scheduled posts.\", ex);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Immutable DTO summarizing scheduled-publishing results.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed record ScheduledPublishingSummary(\n        int InspectedPosts,\n        int PublishedPosts,\n        int FailedPosts,\n        TimeSpan Elapsed)\n    {\n        public int PendingPosts => InspectedPosts - (PublishedPosts + FailedPosts);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Exception wrapper for unrecoverable scheduled-publishing errors.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class ScheduledPublishingException : Exception\n    {\n        public throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postRepository));\n            _postPublisher         = postPublisher   ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(postPublisher));\n            _clock                 = clock           ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(clock));\n            _domainEventDispatcher = domainEventDispatcher ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(domainEventDispatcher));\n            _logger                = logger          ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n        }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Publishes all posts whose scheduled publish time has arrived.\n        /// \n        /// Returns the number of posts successfully published.  Individual post\n        /// failures are logged *and swallowed* so that one bad apple does not\n        /// poison the entire batch.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"cancellationToken\">Cancellation for long-running jobs.</param>\n        public async Task<int> ExecuteAsync(CancellationToken cancellationToken = default)\n        {\n            var now = _clock.UtcNow;\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"ScheduledPublishing job started at {UtcNow}\", now);\n\n            IReadOnlyList<Post> duePosts;\n            try\n            {\n                duePosts = await _postRepository\n                    .GetPostsScheduledForPublishingAsync(now, cancellationToken)\n                    .ConfigureAwait(false);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex)\n            {\n                _logger.LogError(ex, \"Unable to query repository for scheduled posts.\");\n                throw; // Fail-fast\u2014this indicates infrastructure outage.\n            }\n\n            if (duePosts.Count == 0)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"No posts due for publishing at {UtcNow}.\", now);\n                return 0;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Found {PostCount} post(s) scheduled for publishing.\", duePosts.Count);\n\n            var publishCount = 0;\n            foreach (var post in duePosts)\n            {\n                if (cancellationToken.IsCancellationRequested)\n                {\n                    _logger.LogWarning(\"Cancellation requested, aborting remaining publishes.\");\n                    break;\n                }\n\n                try\n                {\n                    await PublishPostAsync(post, cancellationToken).ConfigureAwait(false);\n                    publishCount++;\n                }\n                catch (Exception ex)\n                {\n                    // Swallow exception for individual posts; surfaces via logging/observability.\n                    _logger.LogError(ex,\n                        \"Failed to publish PostId={PostId}, slug '{Slug}'. Continuing with next item.\",\n                        post.PostId,\n                        post.Slug);\n                }\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"ScheduledPublishing job completed. {Published} / {Total} posts published.\",\n                publishCount, duePosts.Count);\n\n            return publishCount;\n        }\n\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n        // Internal helpers\n        // ---------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n        private async Task PublishPostAsync(Post post, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            // Double-check to protect against race conditions: another worker\n            // might have already published this post in the meantime.\n            if (post.Status == PostStatus.Published)\n            {\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"PostId={PostId} already published by another instance.\", post.PostId);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // Domain rule: A post cannot be published if it is awaiting approval\n            // by an editor.  Handle gracefully.\n            if (post.RequiresApproval && !post.IsApproved)\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(\"PostId={PostId} requires approval and will not be auto-published.\", post.PostId);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Publishing PostId={PostId} (slug '{Slug}').\", post.PostId, post.Slug);\n\n            // 1) Delegate to the publishing adapter (e.g., markdown \u2192 HTML).\n            await _postPublisher.PublishAsync(post, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // 2) Update repository state.\n            post.MarkAsPublished(_clock.UtcNow);\n            await _postRepository.UpdateAsync(post, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            // 3) Raise domain events (analytics, notifications, etc.).\n            var evt = new PostPublishedEvent(post.PostId, post.PublishedAt!.Value);\n            await _domainEventDispatcher.DispatchAsync(evt, ct).ConfigureAwait(false);\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Successfully published PostId={PostId}.\", post.PostId);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Domain entities & value objects (minimal representation)\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    public enum PostStatus\n    {\n        Draft        = 0,\n        Scheduled    = 1,\n        Published    = 2,\n        Archived     = 3\n    }\n\n    public sealed class Post\n    {\n        private readonly List<object> _domainEvents = new();\n\n        public Guid            PostId        { get; }\n        public string          Slug          { get; }\n        public PostStatus      Status        { get; private set; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishAt     { get; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? PublishedAt   { get; private set; }\n\n        // Simplified approval flags\n        public bool            RequiresApproval { get; }\n        public bool            IsApproved       { get; private set; }\n\n        public IReadOnlyCollection<object> DomainEvents => _domainEvents.AsReadOnly();\n\n        public Post(Guid postId,\n                    string slug,\n                    PostStatus status,\n                    DateTimeOffset? publishAt,\n                    bool requiresApproval,\n                    bool isApproved)\n        {\n            PostId           = postId;\n            Slug             = slug;\n            Status           = status;\n            PublishAt        = publishAt;\n            RequiresApproval = requiresApproval;\n            IsApproved       = isApproved;\n        }\n\n        public void Approve()\n        {\n            if (!RequiresApproval)\n                throw new InvalidOperationException(\"Approval not required.\");\n\n            if (IsApproved)\n                return;\n\n            IsApproved = true;\n            AddDomainEvent(new PostApprovedEvent(PostId, DateTimeOffset.UtcNow));\n        }\n\n        public void MarkAsPublished(DateTimeOffset publishedAt)\n        {\n            if (Status == PostStatus.Published)\n                return;\n\n            Status      = PostStatus.Published;\n            PublishedAt = publishedAt;\n            AddDomainEvent(new PostStatusChangedEvent(PostId, Status, publishedAt));\n        }\n\n        private void AddDomainEvent(object @event) => _domainEvents.Add(@event);\n    }\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Domain Events\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    public sealed record PostPublishedEvent(Guid PostId, DateTimeOffset PublishedAt);\n    public sealed record PostApprovedEvent(Guid PostId, DateTimeOffset ApprovedAt);\n    public sealed record PostStatusChangedEvent(Guid PostId, PostStatus Status, DateTimeOffset ChangedAt);\n\n    // ========================================================================\n    // Ports (Interfaces) \u2011 to be implemented by Adapters\n    // ========================================================================\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Time abstraction to decouple from DateTime.UtcNow.\n    /// Allows deterministic tests & time-travel simulations.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface ISystemClock\n    {\n        DateTimeOffset UtcNow { get; }\n    }\n\n    public interface IPostRepository\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Returns every post whose <c>PublishAt</c> \u2264 <paramref name=\"asOf\"/> and\n        /// whose status is <see cref=\"PostStatus.Scheduled\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task<IReadOnlyList<Post>> GetPostsScheduledForPublishingAsync(\n            DateTimeOffset asOf,\n            CancellationToken cancellationToken);\n\n        Task UpdateAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Responsible for turning a <see cref=\"Post\"/> into published content.\n    /// Implementation examples: \u2011 Generate full HTML & push to CDN\n    ///                           \u2011 Enqueue a static-site rebuild\n    ///                           \u2011 Call headless CMS API\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IPostPublisher\n    {\n        Task PublishAsync(Post post, CancellationToken cancellationToken);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Dispatches domain events (Sync or Async).\n    /// Typical implementation: wraps MediatR, NATS, Kafka, etc.\n    /// </summary>\n    public interface IDomainEventDispatcher\n    {\n        Task DispatchAsync(object domainEvent, CancellationToken cancellationToken);\n    }\n}\n```",

The implementation demonstrates:\n//\n//  \u2022 Strict adherence to Hexagonal Architecture \u2013 depends only on ports, never on other\n//    concrete adapters.\n//\n//  \u2022 Caching via IDistributedCache (Redis, Mem-cached, in-memory) to avoid re-aggregating\n//    frequently requested ranges.\n//\n//  \u2022 Resilience via Polly for transient SQL and cache faults.\n//\n//  \u2022 (Adapter) ================================================\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Hexagonal adapter that builds <see cref=\"EditorialAnalyticsReport\"/> instances\n    /// from the underlying analytics database and caches them for future calls.\n    /// </summary>\n    public sealed class EditorialAnalyticsService : IEditorialAnalyticsService\n    {\n        private const string CacheKeyTemplate = \"analytics:{0:yyyyMMddHHmm}:{1:yyyyMMddHHmm}:{2}\";\n        private static readonly JsonSerializerOptions _jsonOptions = new(JsonSerializerDefaults.Web);\n\n        private readonly IPostAnalyticsRepository _repository;\n        private readonly IDistributedCache _cache;\n        private readonly ILogger<EditorialAnalyticsService> _logger;\n        private readonly AsyncRetryPolicy _retryPolicy;\n\n        public EditorialAnalyticsService(\n            IPostAnalyticsRepository repository,\n            IDistributedCache cache,\n            ILogger<EditorialAnalyticsService> logger)\n        {\n            _repository = repository ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(repository));\n            _cache = cache ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(cache));\n            _logger = logger ?? throw new ArgumentNullException(nameof(logger));\n\n            // Simple Polly retry for transient faults (SQL, Redis, etc.)\n            _retryPolicy = Policy\n                .Handle<Exception>(ex => IsTransient(ex))\n                .WaitAndRetryAsync(\n                    retryCount: 3,\n                    sleepDurationProvider: attempt => TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(100 * attempt),\n                    onRetry: (ex, span, attempt, ctx) =>\n                    {\n                        _logger.LogWarning(ex,\n                            \"Transient failure when computing editorial analytics. Retrying {Attempt}/3 after {Delay}ms\",\n                            attempt,\n                            span.TotalMilliseconds);\n                    });\n        }\n\n        public async Task<EditorialAnalyticsReport> BuildAsync(\n            DateTime fromUtc,\n            DateTime toUtc,\n            AnalyticsGranularity granularity,\n            CancellationToken ct = default)\n        {\n            if (fromUtc >= toUtc)\n                throw new ArgumentException(\"'fromUtc' must be earlier than 'toUtc'.\");\n\n            string cacheKey = GetCacheKey(fromUtc, toUtc, granularity);\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Attempting to retrieve analytics report from cache using key {CacheKey}\", cacheKey);\n\n            // Try cache first \u2013 read-as-fast-as-possible, never fail the request if cache is unavailable.\n            EditorialAnalyticsReport? cachedReport = await TryReadFromCacheAsync(cacheKey, ct);\n            if (cachedReport is not null)\n            {\n                _logger.LogInformation(\"Analytics report served from cache ({CacheKey})\", cacheKey);\n                return cachedReport;\n            }\n\n            _logger.LogInformation(\"Cache miss for analytics report ({CacheKey}). Building from repository\u2026\", cacheKey);\n\n            // Build with retry resilience.\n            EditorialAnalyticsReport report = await _retryPolicy.ExecuteAsync(\n                async token => await BuildInternalAsync(fromUtc, toUtc, granularity, token),\n                ct);\n\n            // Fire-and-forget cache set (do not await to avoid delaying response).\n            _ = CacheReportAsync(cacheKey, report, ct);\n\n            return report;\n        }\n\n        #region === Internals ===========================================================================\n\n        private static bool IsTransient(Exception ex)\n        {\n            // In a real code base, inspect SqlException numbers, RedisConnectionException, etc.\n            // Here, treat all exceptions as transient for demo purposes.\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        private static string GetCacheKey(DateTime fromUtc, DateTime toUtc, AnalyticsGranularity granularity)\n            => string.Format(CacheKeyTemplate, fromUtc, toUtc, granularity.ToString().ToLowerInvariant());\n\n        private async Task<EditorialAnalyticsReport?> TryReadFromCacheAsync(string cacheKey, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                byte[]? bytes = await _cache.GetAsync(cacheKey, ct);\n                if (bytes is null)\n                    return null;\n\n                var report = JsonSerializer.Deserialize<EditorialAnalyticsReport>(bytes, _jsonOptions);\n                return report;\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex))\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Failed to read analytics report from cache. Skipping.\");\n                return null;\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task CacheReportAsync(string cacheKey, EditorialAnalyticsReport report, CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            try\n            {\n                byte[] bytes = JsonSerializer.SerializeToUtf8Bytes(report, _jsonOptions);\n\n                var options = new DistributedCacheEntryOptions\n                {\n                    AbsoluteExpirationRelativeToNow = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(30),\n                    SlidingExpiration = TimeSpan.FromMinutes(10)\n                };\n\n                await _cache.SetAsync(cacheKey, bytes, options, ct);\n                _logger.LogDebug(\"Analytics report cached under key {CacheKey}\", cacheKey);\n            }\n            catch (Exception ex) when (IsTransient(ex))\n            {\n                _logger.LogWarning(ex, \"Failed to store analytics report in cache.\");\n            }\n        }\n\n        private async Task<EditorialAnalyticsReport> BuildInternalAsync(\n            DateTime fromUtc,\n            DateTime toUtc,\n            AnalyticsGranularity granularity,\n            CancellationToken ct)\n        {\n            IReadOnlyList<PostAnalyticsDto> posts =\n                await _repository.GetPostsAsync(fromUtc, toUtc, ct);\n\n            _logger.LogDebug(\"Fetched {Count} posts from analytics repository\", posts.Count);\n\n            // Bucket posts by chosen granularity.\n            var grouped = posts\n                .GroupBy(p => GetBucketKey(p.PublishedAtUtc, granularity))\n                .OrderBy(g => g.Key);\n\n            List<TimeSlice> slices = new();\n\n            foreach (IGrouping<DateTime, PostAnalyticsDto> bucket in grouped)\n            {\n                int postsPublished = bucket.Count();\n                int words = bucket.Sum(p => p.WordCount);\n                double avgReadTime = bucket.Any() ? bucket.Average(p => p.EstimatedReadTimeSeconds) : 0.0;\n\n                // Flatten tags for popularity metric.\n                var topTags = bucket\n                    .SelectMany(p => p.Tags)\n                    .GroupBy(t => t.ToLowerInvariant())\n                    .Select(g => new TagMetric(g.Key, g.Count()))\n                    .OrderByDescending(t => t.PostCount)\n                    .ThenBy(t => t.Tag)\n                    .Take(5)\n                    .ToList();\n\n                slices.Add(new TimeSlice(\n                    PeriodStartUtc: bucket.Key,\n                    PostsPublished: postsPublished,\n                    WordsAuthored: words,\n                    AvgReadTimeSeconds: Math.Round(avgReadTime, 2),\n                    TopTags: topTags));\n            }\n\n            return new EditorialAnalyticsReport(\n                Slices: slices,\n                GeneratedBy: Environment.MachineName,\n                GeneratedAtUtc: DateTime.UtcNow);\n        }\n\n        private static DateTime GetBucketKey(DateTime timestampUtc, AnalyticsGranularity granularity) =>\n            granularity switch\n            {\n                AnalyticsGranularity.Daily   => timestampUtc.Date,\n                AnalyticsGranularity.Weekly  => ISOWeek.ToDateTime(ISOWeek.GetYear(timestampUtc),\n                                                                   ISOWeek.GetWeekOfYear(timestampUtc), DayOfWeek.Monday),\n                AnalyticsGranularity.Monthly => new DateTime(timestampUtc.Year, timestampUtc.Month, 1, 0, 0, 0, DateTimeKind.Utc),\n                _ => throw new ArgumentOutOfRangeException(nameof(granularity), granularity, null)\n            };\n        #endregion\n    }\n\n    #endregion\n}\n```",

Failures)\n{\n    public static PublishingReport Empty =>\n        new(0, 0, 0, 0, Array.Empty<PublishingFailure>());\n}\n\n/// <summary>\n/// Contains information about a specific post that failed to publish.\n/// </summary>\npublic sealed record PublishingFailure(PostId PostId, string Reason, Exception? Exception);\n\n/// <inheritdoc />\ninternal sealed class ScheduledPublishingService : IScheduledPublishingService\n{\n    private readonly IPostRepository _postRepository;\n    private readonly IUnitOfWork _unitOfWork;\n    private readonly IClock _clock;\n    private readonly IMonetizationRuleEvaluator _monetizationRuleEvaluator;\n    private readonly IDomainEventDispatcher _eventDispatcher;\n    private readonly ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> _logger;\n\n    public ScheduledPublishingService(\n        IPostRepository postRepository,\n        IUnitOfWork unitOfWork,\n        IClock clock,\n        IMonetizationRuleEvaluator monetizationRuleEvaluator,\n        IDomainEventDispatcher eventDispatcher,\n        ILogger<ScheduledPublishingService> logger)\n    {\n        _postRepository           = postRepository ?? Examined={Examined} Published={Published} Skipped={Skipped} Failed={Failed}\",\n            report.TotalExamined, report.SuccessfullyPublished, report.SkippedByRule, report.Failed);\n\n        return report;\n    }\n}\n\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n// Port Definitions (simplified).  In a larger solution these reside in their\n// dedicated namespaces/files but are colocated here for single-file delivery.\n// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\nnamespace TempoScribePro.Domain.Abstractions\n{\n    using System.Threading;\n    using System.Threading.Tasks;\n    using System.Collections.Generic;\n\n    public interface IPostRepository\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Returns every post that is <see cref=\"PostStatus.Scheduled\"/> and whose\n        /// <see cref=\"IPost.ScheduledAt\"/> is earlier or equal to <paramref name=\"utcNow\"/>.\n        /// </summary>\n        Task<IReadOnlyList<IPost>> FindScheduledDueAsync(DateTimeOffset utcNow, CancellationToken token);\n\n        // Other repository members omitted for brevity.\n    }\n\n    public interface IUnitOfWork\n    {\n        Task SaveChangesAsync(CancellationToken token = default);\n    }\n\n    public interface IClock\n    {\n        DateTimeOffset UtcNow { get; }\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Publishes raised domain events to their interested handlers. ScheduledAt { get; private init; }\n        public DateTimeOffset? AddError($\"Cannot publish post in status '{Status}'.\");\n\n        if (ScheduledPublishAtUtc is not null && publishTimestampUtc < ScheduledPublishAtUtc.Value)\n            AddError(\"Attempted to
